# Public Theorem Index вАФ GraphCanonizationProofs

Index of public Lean theorems, lemmas, and definitions in the GraphCanonizationProofs project (active source), grouped by source file path. Archived counterparts live in `Archive/PublicTheoremIndex.md`. Private declarations live in `PrivateTheoremIndex.md`.

Maintained by `scripts/GenerateTheoremIndexes.py rewrite --with-line-numbers`: the **Name**, **Line**, and **Notes** columns are computed from source; **Description** is hand-written and preserved. Prose between tables (this note, the Legend, `### вА¶` sub-headers, per-file descriptions) is passed through untouched.
## Legend

- **Line**: Source-line range `start-end` covering the declaration's header (attached doc comment / attributes) and its full body. Collapses to a single number when the declaration occupies one line. Gaps between theorems represent whitespace or comments.
- **Description**: What the declaration achieves / why a consumer would use it (not how it is proved), in вЙ§ 2 sentences. A leading `¬ІвА¶` section marker or **bold anchor** links it to the documentation.
- **Notes**: Computed from source вАФ the infrastructure kind (`Definition`/`Structure`/`Inductive`/`Class`/`abbrev`/`axiom`/`Instance`), `noncomputable`, and `@[вА¶]` attributes. `private` is omitted (it is encoded by the public/private index split).

## ChainDescent.lean

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `POE` | 76-80 | Partial-order entries: the three values `less`, `unknown`, `greater` that populate a `PMatrix`. | Inductive |
| `neg` | 93-97 | Antisymmetric reverse on one entry: swaps `less`/`greater`, fixes `unknown`. | Definition |
| `neg_neg` | 99-100 | `neg` is an involution: `neg (neg e) = e`. | `@[simp]` |
| `POE.swap` | 102-105 | ѕГ-swap on one entry (the matrix-wide relabelling of the direction-symmetry argument); coincides with `neg`. | Definition |
| `POE.swap_swap` | 107 | ѕГ-swap is an involution: `swap (swap e) = e`. | `@[simp]` |
| `swap_less` | 109 | `swap .less = .greater`. | `@[simp]` |
| `swap_greater` | 110 | `swap .greater = .less`. | `@[simp]` |
| `swap_unknown` | 111 | `swap .unknown = .unknown`. | `@[simp]` |
| `PMatrix` | 117-118 | The partial-order matrix type `Fin n вЖТ Fin n вЖТ POE`. | Definition |
| `swap` | 124-125 | Pointwise ѕГ-swap of a `PMatrix`: swap `less` with `greater` at every entry. | Definition |
| `swap_swap` | 127-128 | ѕГ-swap is an involution on `PMatrix`: `swap (swap P) = P`. | `@[simp]` |
| `Antisymmetric` | 130-132 | A `PMatrix` is antisymmetric when `P i j = POE.neg (P j i)` for all `i, j`. | Definition |
| `AdjMatrix` | 141-142 | Self-contained adjacency matrix on `Fin n`, wrapping a `Fin n вЖТ Fin n вЖТ Nat` field. | Structure |
| `applyGuess` | 146-153 | Apply a single guess `(a, b, dir)` to `P`: set `P a b := dir`, `P b a := neg dir`, leaving every other entry unchanged. Does not transitively close. | Definition |
| `closeStep` | 180-193 | Single-step transitive closure: derive `P i j` from a uniform chain `i вЖТ k вЖТ j`, with `less`-chains taking priority over `greater`-chains at ties. | Definition |
| `transitiveClose` | 195-199 | Transitive closure of a `PMatrix` by iterating `closeStep` `n*n` times вАФ enough rounds to reach fixpoint. | Definition |
| `conflictMatrix` | 230-243 | Concrete 4-vertex witness with a conflicted pair `(0,1)` carrying both a `less`-chain and a `greater`-chain; refutes ѕГ-swap commutation. | Definition |
| `closeStep_swap_false` | 262-271 | **Refutation:** `closeStep` does not commute with ѕГ-swap unconditionally вАФ the `less`-first tie-break is not ѕГ-symmetric (fails on `conflictMatrix`). | вАФ |
| `transitiveClose_swap_false` | 292-306 | **Refutation:** `transitiveClose` does not commute with ѕГ-swap unconditionally (witnessed by `conflictMatrix`). | вАФ |
| `Colouring` | 310-311 | A vertex colouring `Fin n вЖТ Nat`. | Definition |
| `signature` | 313-319 | Multiset signature of vertex `v` under colouring `ѕЗ` and state `(adj, P)`: the `(ѕЗ u, adj.adj v u, P v u)` tuples over all `u вЙ† v`. | Definition |
| `POE.toNat` | 321-326 | Numeric code for a `POE` entry matching the C# packing: `less вЖ¶ 0`, `unknown вЖ¶ 1`, `greater вЖ¶ 2`. | Definition |
| `encTuple` | 332-338 | Canonical injection of a signature tuple `(colour, edge-label, POE)` into `Nat` (Cantor pairing); mirrors the C# neighbour-tuple packing. | Definition |
| `sigKey` | 347-354 | Canonical refinement key of a vertex: its old colour followed by the sorted encoded signature multiset (the C# `[own-colour, sorted neighbour-tuples]`). | Definition |
| `sigKey_eq_iff` | 356-370 | Two vertices share a `sigKey` iff they have the same old colour and the same signature. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine` | 399-409 | Warm 1-WL refinement: iterate `refineStep` `n` times from `initial`; concrete and computable. | Definition |
| `refineStep` / `refineStep_iff` | ~320-417 | **Concrete (2026-05-30, no longer axioms):** `refineStep adj P ѕЗ v := Encodable.encode (sigKey adj P ѕЗ v)` (own colour + sorted encoded signature = the C# `WarmPartition.RefineRound`); `refineStep_iff` (same colour вЯЇ same old colour + same signature) is now a **theorem**. Removes `refineStep`/`refineStep_iff` from the axiom basis project-wide. Helpers: `POE.toNat`(_injective), `encTuple`(_injective), `sigKey`, `sigKey_eq_iff`. | Def + theorem |
| `samePartition` | 413-416 | Two colourings induce the same partition: `ѕЗвВБ i = ѕЗвВБ j вЖФ ѕЗвВВ i = ѕЗвВВ j` for every `i, j`. | Definition |
| `samePartition.refl` | 422 | `samePartition` is reflexive. | вАФ |
| `samePartition.symm` | 424-425 | `samePartition` is symmetric. | вАФ |
| `samePartition.trans` | 427-429 | `samePartition` is transitive. | вАФ |
| `refineStep_refines` | 435-440 | **Refinement is split-only (one round).** Equal refined colour implies equal old colour. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_refines` | 442-468 | Warm refinement is split-only: equal warm-refined colour implies equal starting colour. | вАФ |
| `cell_split_uniform_false` | 571-596 | **Refutation:** cell-mates do not in general keep equal signatures after a guess plus TC (witnessed by `witnessP0`, the gap fixed only by singleton-cell `a`, `b`). | вАФ |
| `iterate_refineStep_preserves_singleton` | 627-640 | Iterating refinement preserves a singleton for any number of rounds. | вАФ |
| `signature_eq_of_samePartition` | 658-685 | **Signature equality is a partition invariant of the colouring:** partition-equal colourings induce the same signature-equality relation between vertices. | вАФ |
| `warm_6_2` | 687-764 | **¬І6.2 direction invariance.** With `a, b` `ѕЗќє`-singletons, warm refinement after `a < b` and after `b < a` induce the same partition. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_swap` | 780-822 | **Direction-blindness (Q1).** Warm refinement on `P` and on its ѕГ-swap induce the same partition. | вАФ |
| `applyGuess_comm` | 836-854 | **Q2 вАФ guesses commute.** Guessing on `{a,b}` then `{b,c}` (pairwise-distinct vertices) gives the same `(adj, P)` as the reverse order, since the writes touch disjoint matrix entries. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_agree_off'` | 875-922 | **¬І6.2 вАФ composable cross-branch sharing.** Matrices agreeing off `D` and `samePartition`-equal starting colourings (with `D` all `ѕЗ`-singletons) yield the same warm-refined partition; the cross-level form that chains across descent levels. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_agree_off` | 924-958 | **¬І6.2 вАФ the cell partition depends only on the matrix off the decision set `D`.** Matrices agreeing off `D` (its vertices `ѕЗќє`-singletoned) yield the same partition; the same-`ѕЗќє` specialisation of `warmRefine_agree_off'`. | вАФ |
| `PartitionInvariant` | 975-979 | A target-cell selector is partition-invariant when it depends only on the partition a colouring induces, not on raw colour values. | Definition |
| `target_direction_blind` | 981-990 | **¬І6.2 spine вАФ base case.** For a partition-invariant selector, the target cell chosen after `a < b` equals the one after `b < a`. | вАФ |
| `target_agree_off` | 992-1005 | **¬І6.2 spine вАФ inductive step.** For a partition-invariant selector and matrices agreeing off a singletoned decision set `D`, the target cell is the same even when the start colourings only agree up to partition. | вАФ |
| `Egnd` | 1034-1035 | **¬І13.** The canonical ground set on `Fin n`: ordered pairs `(i, j)` with `i < j`. | Definition |
| `Pof` | 1043-1056 | **¬І13.** Commit a set `S вКЖ Egnd n` of pair-guesses into a P-matrix: write `less` at `(u,v) вИИ S`, `greater` at `(v,u)`, leaving other entries unchanged. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `cl` | 1058-1063 | **¬І13.** Propagation closure on pair-guesses: the canonical pairs whose endpoints get separated by warm refinement after committing `S`. | Definition |
| `SingletonAt` | 1073-1075 | The fresh-colour hypothesis at a pair `p`: both `p.1` and `p.2` are `ѕЗќє`-singletons. | Definition |
| `cl_extensive` | 1077-1092 | **¬І13 M1 вАФ extensiveness of `cl`.** For canonical `S` whose vertices are all `ѕЗќє`-singletons, every pair in `S` lies in `cl S`. | вАФ |
| `FullyDiscrete` | 1158-1160 | A colouring is fully discrete when every vertex is its own `ѕЗќє`-singleton. | Definition |
| `cl_monotone_discrete` | 1162-1179 | **¬І13 M0, vacuous case.** Under `FullyDiscrete`, every canonical pair lies in every `cl S`, so `cl S = Egnd n` and monotonicity carries no structural information. | вАФ |
| `TVerticesSingletons` | 1192-1194 | Every endpoint of every pair in `T` is a `ѕЗќє`-singleton. | Definition |
| `warmRefine_samePartition_T_individualised` | 1196-1281 | **¬І13 M0, strong form.** Warm refinement under `Pof PвВА S` and `Pof PвВА T` induces the *same* partition when `S вКЖ T` and every endpoint of every `T`-pair is a `ѕЗќє`-singleton. | вАФ |
| `cl_monotone_T_individualised` | 1283-1294 | **¬І13 M0 вАФ monotonicity of `cl`** under the T-individualised hypothesis: `S вКЖ T` implies `cl S вКЖ cl T`. | вАФ |
| `cl_idempotent` | 1320-1334 | **¬І13 M2 вАФ idempotence of `cl`** under fresh-colour individualisation of `S вИ™ cl S`: `cl (cl S) = cl S`. | вАФ |
| `Pof_fs` | 1406-1412 | **¬І14.** Finset-based computable analogue of `Pof`, enabling `decide`-checkable refutations. | Definition |
| `commitsToP` | 1414-1416 | **¬І14.** All-unknown-base commits-to-matrix shortcut: `Pof_fs (fun _ _ => .unknown) S`. | Definition |
| `cl_prov` | 1418-1423 | **¬І14.** Provenance closure (TC-based): the canonical pair-guesses whose direction is decided by `transitiveClose` of `commitsToP S`. | Definition |
| `cl_prov_empty` | 1454-1463 | **¬І14 CL0 for `cl_prov`:** `cl_prov вИЕ = вИЕ`. | вАФ |
| `cl_prov_extensive` | 1465-1479 | **¬І14 CL1 for `cl_prov`:** for canonical `S`, every commit's direct `less` write survives transitive closure, so `S вКЖ cl_prov S`. | вАФ |
| `cl_prov_M3_false` | 1497-1507 | **¬І14 вАФ refutes matroid M3 exchange for `cl_prov`.** A concrete `n=5, S={(1,2),(3,4)}, x=(2,3), y=(1,4)` counterexample where the M3 premise holds but the conclusion fails; machine-checked by `decide`. | вАФ |
| `hasLessChain` | 1521-1524 | Existence of a `.less`-chain in `P` from `i` to `j` via some intermediate `k` with both edges `.less`. | Definition |
| `hasGreaterChain` | 1526-1528 | Existence of a `.greater`-chain in `P` from `i` to `j` via some intermediate `k`. | Definition |
| `CanConsistent` | 1530-1534 | A `PMatrix` is canonical-consistent when every `.less` entry sits at `i.val < j.val` and every `.greater` entry at `i.val > j.val`. | Definition |
| `LessMono` | 1536-1539 | One-sided `.less`-direction entry-wise monotonicity between two matrices: `P i j = .less вЖТ Q i j = .less`. | Definition |
| `cl_prov_monotone` | 1809-1834 | **¬І14 CL3 вАФ monotonicity for `cl_prov`:** canonical `S вКЖ T` implies `cl_prov S вКЖ cl_prov T`. | вАФ |
| `numUnknown` | 1843-1846 | Number of `.unknown` entries in a `PMatrix` вАФ the strictly-decreasing potential bounding TC iteration. | Definition |
| `transitiveClose_idempotent` | 1974-1980 | **TC idempotence.** `transitiveClose (transitiveClose M) = transitiveClose M`. | вАФ |
| `cl_prov_idempotent` | 2011-2041 | **CL2 вАФ idempotence.** `cl_prov (cl_prov S) = cl_prov S` for canonical `S`. | вАФ |
| `IndivStep` | 2128-2152 | Existential witness of one descent-step individualisation: a colouring `ѕЗ'` that singletons every vertex in target `T` and refines `ѕЗ` outside `T`. Data, not a function вАФ the trace carries one per step. | Structure |
| `singletons_union` | 2156-2177 | **D-singletons preserved.** If `ѕЗ` singletons every `v вИИ D`, an `IndivStep` with target `T` singletons every `v вИИ D вИ™ T`. | вАФ |
| `IndivStep.default` | 2211-2262 | **Concrete `IndivStep` witness.** A constructive individualisation step (parity-tagged base-`n` encoding), proving traces exist at every level so the spine theorem is non-vacuous. | Definition |
| `DescentTrace` | 2271-2309 | Inductive predicate: `(D, P, ѕЗќє)` is reachable by `k` descent steps from `(PвВА, ѕЗќєвВА)` under selector `sel`, each step carrying an `IndivStep` witness and a matrix agreeing with `PвВА` off the enlarged decision set. | Inductive |
| `singletons` | 2313-2330 | **Trace invariant.** A trace's colouring singletons its whole decision set `D`. | вАФ |
| `P_agrees` | 2332-2342 | **Trace invariant.** A trace's matrix agrees with `PвВА` on every entry with an endpoint outside `D`. | вАФ |
| `SpineChain` | 2346-2354 | Bundle of a `DescentTrace` with its derived state `(D, P, ѕЗќє)`. The spine theorem is branch-independence of two such chains. | Structure |
| `partition` | 2361-2365 | The chain's level-`k` partition: warm refinement of its accumulated `(P, ѕЗќє)`. | Definition |
| `spine_branch_independent` | 2386-2460 | **The spine theorem (branch independence).** Any two `DescentTrace`s through `k` levels agree on the accumulated `D` (literal) and the level-`k` partition (`samePartition`) вАФ handing the oracle one fixed partition instead of `2^d` refinement worlds. | вАФ |
| `SpineChain.branch_independent` | 2462-2471 | **The spine theorem, `SpineChain` wrapper.** Two chains at level `k` share `D` and level-`k` partition. | вАФ |
| `defaultColouring` | 2492-2502 | The level-`k` colouring of the default reference chain: iterate refine-then-individualise (via `IndivStep.default`) from `ѕЗќєвВА`, with the matrix held fixed at `PвВА`. | Definition |
| `defaultD` | 2504-2513 | The level-`k` decision set of the default chain: accumulate `sel (warmRefine adj PвВА (defaultColouring k))` across all levels. | Definition |
| `defaultTrace` | 2515-2528 | The concrete `DescentTrace` realising the default construction, using `IndivStep.default` at every level and `P = PвВА` throughout. | Definition |
| `defaultSpineChain` | 2530-2538 | The concrete reference `SpineChain` at every level, bundling `defaultD`/`PвВА`/`defaultColouring`/`defaultTrace`. | Definition |
| `SpineChain.eq_default` | 2540-2551 | **Reference corollary.** Every `SpineChain` at level `k` shares `D` and level-`k` partition with `defaultSpineChain` вАФ there is a canonical level-`k` partition, computable by one deterministic descent. | вАФ |
| `Discrete` | 2575-2578 | A colouring is discrete when every cell is a singleton вАФ equivalently, `ѕЗ : Fin n вЖТ Nat` is injective. | Definition |
| `of_samePartition` | 2582-2586 | Discreteness is `samePartition`-invariant: equal partitions transport `Discrete`. | вАФ |
| `SpineChain.IsLeaf` | 2601-2607 | A `SpineChain` reaches a leaf when its level-`k` partition is discrete (every vertex a singleton). | Definition |
| `TargetsNonsingletonCell` | 2622-2628 | Selector hypothesis: every returned vertex has a same-colour partner (`sel` only picks from non-singleton cells). | Definition |
| `NonemptyOnNonDiscrete` | 2630-2635 | Selector hypothesis: `sel ѕЗ` is non-empty whenever `ѕЗ` is not yet discrete. | Definition |
| `defaultD_univ_isLeaf` | 2637-2652 | **`D` covers all vertices вЗТ leaf.** When the accumulated decision set is the full vertex set, the default chain's spine partition is discrete. | вАФ |
| `defaultD_grows_if_not_leaf` | 2654-2693 | **`D` strictly grows on every non-leaf step.** Under the two selector hypotheses, a non-leaf level-`k` chain has `|defaultD k| < |defaultD (k+1)|`. | вАФ |
| `defaultSpineChain_reaches_leaf` | 2695-2734 | **Leaf existence.** Under `TargetsNonsingletonCell` and `NonemptyOnNonDiscrete`, the default descent reaches a leaf within `n` levels. | вАФ |
| `DirAssignment` | 2757-2763 | Order assignment relative to `(PвВА, D)`: an antisymmetric matrix agreeing with `PвВА` on every entry with an endpoint outside `D`. The linear oracle's input shape вАФ a point in the order-label residual. | Structure |
| `default` | 2769-2776 | **Trivial `DirAssignment`.** When `PвВА` is antisymmetric, `PвВА` itself is a valid order assignment for any `D` (witnesses non-emptiness). | Definition |
| `samePartition_pair` | 2778-2790 | Any two `DirAssignment`s over the same `(PвВА, D)`, refined against a `D`-singletoning colouring, induce the same partition. | вАФ |
| `samePartition_chain` | 2792-2805 | **Spine equivalence.** A `DirAssignment` over a chain's `D`, refined against the chain's colouring, induces the chain's partition вАФ the residual is exactly the choice of `DirAssignment`, partition fixed. | вАФ |
| `flipPair` | 2809-2853 | **Single-pair direction flip.** Negate the `(a, b)` and `(b, a)` entries of a `DirAssignment` via `POE.neg`. The generator of the `ZвВВ` group action on direction choices. | Definition |
| `flipPair_idempotent` | 2867-2876 | **Flip is an involution.** Two applications of `flipPair` to the same pair return the original `DirAssignment` вАФ the `ZвВВ` generator squares to identity. | вАФ |
| `flipPair_partition_invariant` | 2878-2888 | **Flipping preserves the partition.** `ѕГ` and `ѕГ.flipPair a b` share the spine partition вАФ the order labels move, the partition doesn't. | вАФ |
| `flipPair_comm` | 2890-2914 | **Flips on disjoint pairs commute** вАФ the abelian-ness of the `ZвВВ^d` action: distinct decisions don't interfere. | вАФ |
| `IsAut` | 2942-2945 | A `Fin n`-permutation `ѕА` is a graph automorphism of `adj` when it preserves adjacency edge-by-edge: `adj.adj (ѕА v) (ѕА w) = adj.adj v w`. | Definition |
| `IsAut.refl` | 2951-2952 | The identity permutation is an automorphism. | вАФ |
| `IsAut.trans` | 2954-2959 | Composition of automorphisms is an automorphism. | вАФ |
| `IsAut.symm` | 2961-2967 | The inverse of an automorphism is an automorphism. | вАФ |
| `labelledAdj` | 2971-2977 | **Labelled adjacency.** Adjacency matrix relabelled by `ѕА`: entry `(i, j)` is the original adjacency between `ѕАвБї¬є i` and `ѕАвБї¬є j`. | Definition |
| `labelledAdj_eq_of_isAut` | 2979-2992 | **Automorphisms fix the labelled adjacency.** `IsAut ѕА adj` implies `labelledAdj ѕА adj = adj.adj` вАФ an automorphism is invisible at the labelled level. | вАФ |
| `isAut_of_labelledAdj_eq` | 2994-3004 | **Converse.** A permutation preserving the labelled adjacency is an automorphism. | вАФ |
| `vertexRankNat` | 3017-3019 | Strict rank of vertex `v`: the count of vertices `u` with `ѕЗ u < ѕЗ v`. | Definition |
| `vertexRank` | 3037-3039 | Vertex rank packaged as `Fin n` via `vertexRankNat_lt_n`. | Definition |
| `rankPerm` | 3079-3083 | **The rank permutation.** Bijection `Fin n вЙГ Fin n` mapping each vertex to its colour-rank on a `Discrete` colouring. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `rankPerm_apply` | 3085-3086 | Unfolding lemma: `rankPerm ѕЗ h v = vertexRank ѕЗ v`. | `@[simp]` |
| `vertexRank_comp` | 3090-3109 | `vertexRank (ѕЗ вИШ g) v = vertexRank ѕЗ (g v)` вАФ a pure `Finset.card` reindex along `g`. *(Relocated from `LinearOracle.lean` for the cascade oracle's `colourMatchPerm` (M-B).)* | вАФ |
| `rankPerm_comp` | 3111-3131 | **Rank reindexing.** `rankPerm (ѕЗ вИШ e) = rankPerm ѕЗ ¬Ј e` вАФ relabelling conjugate-shifts the rank permutation (the ¬ІL.5 conjugation gap). *(Relocated from `LinearOracle.lean`.)* | вАФ |
| `SpineChain.canonAdj` | 3147-3173 | **Leaf canonical adjacency.** Given a leaf `SpineChain` and a `DirAssignment ѕГ` over its `D`, relabel `adj` by the rank permutation of the warm-refined partition. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `matrixLT` | 3177-3184 | **Row-major lex strict less-than on `n √Ч n` matrices.** The first disagreeing cell `(i, j)` (row-then-column order) has `MвВБ i j < MвВВ i j`. | Definition |

| `DirAssignment.fintype` | 3227-3237 | **`Fintype` on `DirAssignment PвВА D`.** Obtained by injecting the ѕГ-field into the `Fintype` `PMatrix n`. | Instance, `noncomputable` |
| `relabelMatrix` | 3241-3248 | **Relabel a bare matrix** `Fin n вЖТ Fin n вЖТ Nat` by a permutation `ѕА`: entry `(i,j)` becomes `M (ѕАвБї¬є i) (ѕАвБї¬є j)`. Lets `LeafTwistSpec` state the leaf-relabelling property without re-wrapping as an `AdjMatrix`. | Definition |
| `MatrixLex` | 3250-3255 | `Fin n вЖТ Fin n вЖТ Nat` viewed under the row-major lex order via nested `Pi.Lex`. | `abbrev` |

| `canonForm` | 3297-3317 | **The canonical leaf adjacency matrix:** the lex-min `canonAdj` over all `DirAssignment`s (row-major lex). Requires `Nonempty (DirAssignment PвВА chain.D)`. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `canonForm_mem_image` | 3319-3334 | **`canonForm` comes from some `DirAssignment`:** it equals `canonAdj ѕГ` for some `ѕГ`. | вАФ |
| `canonForm_le_canonAdj` | 3336-3352 | **`canonForm` is the lex-minimum:** `toMatrixLex (canonForm) вЙ§ toMatrixLex (canonAdj ѕГ)` for every `DirAssignment ѕГ`. | вАФ |
| `LinearOracleSpec` | 3356-3372 | **The linear-oracle interface type:** given a leaf chain and a current-branch `DirAssignment`, return either `none` or a verified automorphism of `adj` (bundled as a subtype). | Definition |
| `some_isAut` | 3379-3391 | **Soundness (subtype-level):** when the oracle returns `some result`, the returned permutation is automatically an automorphism. | вАФ |
| `LeafTwistSpec` | 3393-3410 | **Leaf-twist validity spec:** when the oracle returns `some result`, the returned `ѕА` relabels the input branch's canonical adjacency to that of some other `DirAssignment ѕГ'` вАФ the property justifying pruning. | Definition |
| `individualizedColouring` | 3448-3452 | **Fresh-colour individualisation** of a vertex set `S`: each `v вИИ S` gets unique colour `v.val + 1`; vertices outside `S` share colour `0`. | Definition |
| `FixesPointwise` | 3454-3457 | Predicate: permutation `ѕА` fixes every vertex in `S` pointwise (`ѕА v = v` for `v вИИ S`). | Definition |
| `complement` | 3463-3471 | A pointwise-fixing permutation stabilises the complement setwise: `v вИЙ S` implies `ѕА v вИЙ S`. | вАФ |
| `individualizedColouring_invariant` | 3475-3484 | An automorphism fixing `S` pointwise preserves the individualised colouring: `ѕЗ_S (ѕА v) = ѕЗ_S v` for every `v`. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_invariant_of_isAut` | 3560-3569 | Warm refinement preserves automorphism invariance: if `(adj, P, ѕЗ_init)` are all `ѕА`-invariant, so is `warmRefine adj P ѕЗ_init`. | вАФ |
| `signature_transport` | 3583-3608 | **Signature transport.** An automorphism `g` carrying `(PвВБ, ѕЗвВБ)` to `(PвВВ, ѕЗвВВ)` maps the `(PвВВ, ѕЗвВВ)`-signature at `g v` to the `(PвВБ, ѕЗвВБ)`-signature at `v`. Cross-config form of `signature_invariant_of_isAut`. | вАФ |
| `sigKey_transport` | 3610-3617 | **`sigKey` transport** вАФ cross-config: `sigKey adj PвВВ ѕЗвВВ (g v) = sigKey adj PвВБ ѕЗвВБ v`. | вАФ |
| `refineStep_transport` | 3619-3627 | **`refineStep` transport** вАФ one round, cross-config: `refineStep adj PвВВ ѕЗвВВ (g v) = refineStep adj PвВБ ѕЗвВБ v`. | вАФ |
| `iterate_refineStep_transport` | 3629-3643 | **Iterated `refineStep` transport** across any number of rounds, cross-config. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_transport` | 3645-3654 | **Warm-refinement transport.** An automorphism carrying `(PвВБ, ѕЗвВБ)` to `(PвВВ, ѕЗвВВ)` carries the warm refinement of the first onto the second. | вАФ |
| `OrbitPartition` | 3670-3676 | **Aut_S orbit relation** on vertices: `v ~ w` iff some automorphism of `adj` preserving `P` and fixing `S` pointwise sends `v` to `w`. | Definition |
| `refl` | 3682-3685 | Reflexivity of `OrbitPartition` (via the identity permutation). | вАФ |
| `symm` | 3687-3702 | Symmetry of `OrbitPartition` (via permutation inverse). | вАФ |
| `trans` | 3704-3719 | Transitivity of `OrbitPartition` (via permutation composition). | вАФ |
| `subset_warmRefine` | 3721-3736 | **Trivial direction of the squeeze:** orbits refine 1-WL cells вАФ `OrbitPartition v w` implies `warmRefine` colours of `v` and `w` agree. | вАФ |
| `refineStep_iter_le_eq` | 3749-3767 | Refinement is split-only across iterations: equality at iterate `k + d` implies equality at iterate `k`. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_eq_iter_eq` | 3769-3783 | `warmRefine` equality implies iterate-`r` equality for any `r вЙ§ n`; the bridge from the fixpoint partition to any earlier-round partition. | вАФ |
| `id_of_discrete_invariant` | 3808-3817 | **Fact B (pointwise):** a `ѕА`-invariant discrete colouring forces `ѕА` to be the identity. | вАФ |
| `aut_trivial_of_discrete_warmRefine` | 3819-3835 | **Fact B (CFI):** if `warmRefine adj P ѕЗ_S` is discrete, every automorphism preserving `(adj, P)` and fixing `S` pointwise is the identity. | вАФ |
| `orbit_iff_eq_of_discrete_warmRefine` | 3837-3855 | **Fact B (partition):** at discrete depth, `OrbitPartition adj P S v w вЖФ v = w`. | вАФ |
| `CascadesAt` | 3877-3884 | **Cascade-at-depth-`k` predicate:** some `S` with `S.card вЙ§ k` makes `warmRefine adj P (individualizedColouring n S)` discrete. | Definition |
| `cascadesAt_univ` | 3886-3905 | **Trivial cascade at depth `n`:** taking `S = univ` gives a discrete starting colouring preserved by warm refinement вАФ the every-graph fallback. | вАФ |
| `theorem_1_HOR_at_depth` | 3925-3948 | **Key theorem (Tier 1 HOR).** If `adj` cascades at depth `k`, some `S` with `S.card вЙ§ k` makes `warmRefine` discrete and the `Aut_S`-orbit partition equal to the `warmRefine` partition. | вАФ |
| `theorem_1_HOR_at_n` | 3970-3981 | **Theorem 1, trivial-bound corollary:** every graph admits orbit recovery at depth `n`. Axiom-free specialisation to `cascadesAt_univ`. | вАФ |
| `theorem_1_HOR` | 3983-3994 | **Theorem 1 (legacy existential form):** some `S` makes `warmRefine` discrete and orbits equal cells. | вАФ |
| `theorem_1_HOR_pointwise` | 3996-4008 | **Theorem 1, pointwise corollary:** at the cascade depth, every automorphism preserving `(adj, P)` and fixing `S` is the identity. | вАФ |
| `SchemeProfile` | 4061-4077 | **Key structure (Tier 2).** Bundles a v-profile colouring with its structural facts: profile classes equal `Aut_v` orbits (schurian Step 1) and 1-WL refines the profile partition (intersection-number Step 2). | Structure |
| `warm_iff_profile` | 4083-4096 | **Squeeze for `SchemeProfile`:** the 1-WL fixpoint partition equals the profile partition. | вАФ |
| `theorem_2_HOR_of_profile` | 4112-4128 | **Theorem 2 (assembly form):** given a `SchemeProfile` witness at `v`, the 1-WL fixpoint partition at depth 1 equals the `Aut_v`-orbit partition. The axiom-free assembly lemma `Scheme.lean`'s `theorem_2_HOR_concrete` consumes (the placeholder axioms `IsSchurianSchemeGraph` / `schurian_scheme_profile_exists` and the conditional `theorem_2_HOR` were retired 2026-06-05). | вАФ |

**¬І15 вАФ Stage 3: gadget-flip automorphisms (the `ZвВВ^ќ≤` generators).** *We build the generator
*existence* (the cycle-space flips), not the full `Aut(CFI) вЙЕ ZвВВ^ќ≤ вЛК Aut(H)` iso вАФ the hard
surjectivity half is needed by no consumer. Both consumers (`LinearOracle.configSwap_of_aut`
and Tier-3a B1's `hwit`) want the same object: a CFI automorphism with controlled support,
realised by the even-subgraph (cycle-space) flip. Phases 0вАУ1 below; Phases 2вАУ6 (adjacency
preservation, `Fin n` lift, support/locality, `P`-preservation, consumer wiring) follow.*

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `card_symmDiff_mod_two` | **Parity helper.** `|S вИЖ T| вЙ° |S| + |T| (mod 2)` вАФ the fact behind "an even subgraph preserves the even-subset invariant." | private |
| `CFIBase.flipSet` | The `F`-incident neighbours of `v` (`F : Fin m вЖТ Fin m вЖТ Bool` an even subgraph), as a subset of `N(v)`. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.symmDiff_flipSet_mem_even` | **Even-subset invariant preserved.** If every `flipSet F v` is even (`F` an even subgraph), `S вИЖ flipSet F v` stays an even subset of `N(v)`. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip` | **The cycle-space gadget flip** on `CFIVertex H`: toggles endpoint parities along `F` (`e^b_{vвЖТw} вЖ¶ e^{bвКХF v w}_{vвЖТw}`) and complements subsets (`a_S^v вЖ¶ a_{S вИЖ flipSet F v}^v`). | Definition (Phase 1) |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_involutive` | The gadget flip is an involution (`(S вИЖ F) вИЖ F = S`; `(bвКХc)вКХc = b`). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlipEquiv` | The gadget flip as an `Equiv.Perm CFIVertex` (self-inverse). | Definition |
| `xor_eq_xor_iff` / `xor_ne_xor_iff` | Xor right-cancellation on `Bool` (`(aвКХc) = (bвКХc) вЖФ a = b`, and the `вЙ†` form). | private |
| `CFIBase.decide_mem_symmDiff_flipSet` | **Phase 2 bridge.** For `w вИИ N(v)`, `w вИИ S вИЖ flipSet F v вЖФ (wвИИS) вКХ F v w` вАФ endpoint parity and subset membership flip together. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_isAut` | **Phase 2 (the automorphism core).** For `F` an even subgraph that is symmetric (`F v w = F w v`), `cfiFlip F` preserves `cfiAdj` on every pair. SubsetвАУendpoint: the `(wвИИS)вКХb` invariant survives the joint flip; endpointвАУendpoint bridge: the single edge `{v,w}` has one `F`-bit (symmetry), so `bвВБ=bвВВ` survives. | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut` | **Phase 3.** The gadget flip transported to `adj`'s vertices `Fin n` via the CFI labelling `h.e`: `g = eвБї¬є вИШ cfiFlip F вИШ e`. | Definition |
| `IsCFI'.e_cfiFlipAut` | Transport identity `e (g v) = cfiFlip F (e v)` вАФ `e` intertwines the `Fin n` and `CFIVertex` flips. | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.isAut_cfiFlipAut` | **Phase-3 deliverable.** For `F` an even symmetric subgraph, `cfiFlipAut F вИИ Aut(adj)` вАФ an honest `IsAut вА¶ adj` (via `matching` + `cfiFlip_isAut`) the consumers (`configSwap_of_aut`, Tier-3a `hwit`) use. | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_involutive` | The lifted flip is an involution (needed where the decision pair must be *swapped*, `g a = b вИІ g b = a`). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.gadget` | **Phase 4.** The base vertex (gadget) of a CFI vertex. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_eq_self_of_flipSet_empty` | **Locality.** If `F` has no edge at `x`'s gadget (`flipSet F (gadget x) = вИЕ`), the flip fixes `x` (`S вИЖ вИЕ = S`; empty flip set вЯє `F v w = false` вЯє parity unchanged). | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_eq_self_of_flipSet_empty` | Locality lifted to `Fin n`: `F` avoiding `i`'s gadget вЯє `cfiFlipAut F` fixes `i`. | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.disjoint_support_cfiFlipAut` | **Phase-4 deliverable.** If every vertex of a committed set `T` lives in an `F`-free gadget, then `Disjoint T (cfiFlipAut F).support` вАФ the exact `Disjoint (committed set) ѕА.support` the path-fixing consumers (`hwit`, `configSwap`) require. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_endpoint` / `_swap` | **C1b.0 recon.** The flip toggles `e^b_{vвЖТw}`'s parity by `F v w`; so it swaps the parity-pair `e^0/e^1` iff `{v,w} вИИ F` вАФ the primary flippable decision pair. | simp / вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_subset` | The flip symmetric-differences `a_S^v` by `flipSet F v` вАФ swaps the subset-pair iff the gadget is `F`-touched (the second flippable kind). | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_endpointVertex` / `_swaps_endpointVertex` | **C1b.0 (lifted).** The `Fin n` swap fact: `cfiFlipAut F` swaps `endpointVertex hw false вЖФ true` iff `F v w = true` вАФ the foundational swap C1b.1 keys on. | вАФ |
| `triFlip_swaps_edge_01` | C1b.0 prototype validation: the triangle flip swaps the parity-pair on edge `{0,1}` (`decide`, independent confirmation). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.isEdgeOf` / `triEdge` | **C1b.2a.** The triangle even-subgraph through edge `{v,w}` with apex `u` вАФ the minimal even subgraph through an edge. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.triEdge_eq_true` / `_iff` / `_symm` / `_cyclic` / `_apex` | Characterisation (membership, source-grouped), symmetry, cyclic invariance `{v,w,u}={w,u,v}`, and `F v w = true`. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_triEdge` / `_other` | The triangle's flip set is `{w,u}` at base vertex `v` (degree 2), and `вИЕ` off `{v,w,u}` (the avoidance вЖТ D-locality). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.triEdge_even` | The triangle is an even subgraph (every vertex F-degree 2 or 0). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.exists_even_triangle` | **C1b.2a deliverable.** If the decision edge has a common neighbour `u` (distinct, in `N(v)вИ©N(w)`), an even symmetric `F` through `{v,w}` exists with support `{v,w,u}` (avoids everything else) вАФ the concrete cycle `F` cascade-1b needs, for triangle-containing bases. General triangle-free bases (KвВГ,вВГ, Petersen) need C1b.2b. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.evenPermEdge` | **C1b.2b.** The even-subgraph indicator of a permutation-cycle `ѕГ` (the cycle's "next-vertex" map). A vertex's F-neighbours are `{ѕГ p, ѕГвБї¬є p}` вАФ degree 2, no list arithmetic. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.evenPermEdge_eq_true` / `_symm` / `_iff_of_mem` | Membership characterisation, symmetry, and the moved-vertex F-neighbours `= {ѕГ p, ѕГвБї¬є p}`. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_evenPermEdge_of_mem` / `_of_fixed` | Flip set `= {ѕГ p, ѕГвБї¬є p}` at a moved vertex (degree 2), `вИЕ` at a fixed point (avoidance). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.evenPermEdge_even` | The permutation-cycle is an even subgraph (degree 2 on the cycle via no-2-cycle, 0 off it). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.exists_even_cycle` | **C1b.2b deliverable.** A permutation-cycle `ѕГ` through `{v,w}` (`ѕГ v = w`) with H-edges (`hEdge`) and orbits вЙ• 3 (`hNo2`) yields an even symmetric `F` through `{v,w}` avoiding every `ѕГ`-fixed vertex. Subsumes the triangle; covers triangle-free bases. The cycle's *existence* in `H вИТ ќ£` is the isolated graph hypothesis (where treewidth enters). | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_preserves_P` | **Phase 5.** The gadget flip preserves any `P` that *every* `adj`-automorphism preserves (the descent's profile/trivial `P`) вАФ transported through `isAut_cfiFlipAut`. Honest scope: a component-moving flip preserves exactly the automorphism-invariant `P`'s. | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_pathFixing_witness` | **Phase-5 deliverable (Tier-3a B1 `hwit` shape).** Assembles Phases 3вАУ5 + `g v = w` into `вИГ ѕА, IsAut ѕА adj вИІ (вИА x u, P (ѕА x)(ѕА u) = P x u) вИІ Disjoint T ѕА.support вИІ ѕА v = w` вАФ exactly what `Cascade.cascadeComposition_pathFixing`'s `hwit` consumes. | вАФ |
| `triFlipEdges` / `triFlip_even` | **Phase-0 prototype:** `triangleBase`'s unique nontrivial even subgraph (all 3 edges; ќ≤=1) and its even-flip-set fact. | Definition / вАФ |
| `triFlip_involutive_check` | Phase-0 smoke test: triangle gadget flip is an involution (`decide`, kernel, axiom-clean). | вАФ |
| `triFlip_isAut_check` | **Phase-0 crux:** the triangle gadget flip preserves `cfiAdj` on all 18√Ч18 pairs (`decide`) вАФ validates cycle-flip-is-automorphism on the smallest case before the general Phase-2 proof. | вАФ |
| `triFlip_nontrivial` | Phase-0 smoke test: the triangle gadget flip moves some vertex вАФ a nontrivial `CFI(triangle)` automorphism. | вАФ |

| `CFIBase.mem_flipSet` | 3262-3265 | Membership in the flip set: `w вИИ flipSet F v вЖФ w вИИ N(v) вИІ F v w`. | `@[simp]` |
| `CFIBase.xorF` | 3293-3295 | **(CFI-cov.2)** Pointwise XOR of two flip-edge indicators вАФ the cycle-space `ZвВВ` sum. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_xorF` | 3297-3305 | **(CFI-cov.2)** The flip-set of an XOR is the symmetric difference of the flip-sets: `flipSet (xorF F F') v = flipSet F v вИЖ flipSet F' v`. The reusable core of the cycle-space sum. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.even_xorF` | 3307-3314 | **(CFI-cov.2)** Even flip-subgraphs stay even under `xorF` (symmetric-difference preserves even cardinality, via `card_symmDiff_mod_two`). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.CycleSpace` | 3316-3319 | **(CFI-cov.2) The cycle space `ZвВВ^ќ≤`**: symmetric, even flip-subgraphs `F` вАФ the index set of the gauge flips `cfiFlip F` (the `ZвВВ^ќ≤` factor of `Aut(CFI(H))`). | Definition |
| `CFIBase.cycleSpace_xorF` | 3321-3324 | **(CFI-cov.2)** The cycle space is closed under the `ZвВВ` sum `xorF` (symmetric + even both preserved). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cycleSpace_const_false` | 3326-3330 | **(CFI-cov.2)** The empty flip-subgraph (zero) lies in the cycle space. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_endpoint_swap` | 3451-3460 | **C1b.0.** The flip swaps the parity-pair `e^0_{vвЖТw}/e^1_{vвЖТw}` iff `F v w = true` (the swap companion of `cfiFlip_endpoint`). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_xorF` | 3478-3493 | **(CFI-cov.3) Gauge flip is a homomorphism on the cycle space:** `cfiFlip (xorF F F') = cfiFlip F вИШ cfiFlip F'` (endpoint: Bool-xor assoc/comm; subset: symmDiff assoc/comm via `flipSet_xorF`). The `ZвВВ^ќ≤`-factor group structure. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_const_false` | 3495-3506 | **(CFI-cov.3)** The zero subgraph is the identity flip: `cfiFlip (fun _ _ => false) = id` (cycle-space zero вЖ¶ identity). | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_triEdge_other` | 3568-3578 | **D-locality.** Off the triangle `{v,w,u}` the triangle's flip set is empty, so the triangle flip fixes every other gadget. | вАФ |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_evenPermEdge_of_fixed` | 3664-3673 | **D-locality (triangle-free bases).** At a `ѕГ`-fixed vertex the permutation-cycle flip set is empty, so the cycle flip avoids every fixed gadget. | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_swaps_endpointVertex` | 3837-3849 | **C1b.0 (lifted to `Fin n`).** `cfiFlipAut F` swaps `endpointVertex hw false вЖФ true` iff `F v w = true` вАФ the foundational decision-pair swap C1b.1 keys on. | вАФ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_xorF` | 3853-3861 | **(CFI-cov.3) The lifted gauge-flip homomorphism:** `cfiFlipAut (xorF F F') = cfiFlipAut F * cfiFlipAut F'` (the `Fin n` form of `cfiFlip_xorF` via `e_cfiFlipAut`). | `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_one` | 3863-3869 | **(CFI-cov.3)** The zero gauge flip is the identity: `cfiFlipAut (fun _ _ => false) = 1` вАФ the homomorphism preserves the unit. | вАФ |

| `AssociationScheme` | 47-91 | A symmetric association scheme on `Fin n`: a partition of `Fin n √Ч Fin n` into `rank + 1` symmetric relations `R_0, вА¶, R_rank` (`R_0` the diagonal) with well-defined intersection numbers `p^k_{ij}`. | Structure |
| `relOfPair` | 107-109 | ¬І1.1 The unique relation index `i : Fin (S.rank + 1)` for which `rel i v w = true`. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `rel_relOfPair` | 111-114 | The pair `(v, w)` lies in `R_{relOfPair v w}`. | вАФ |
| `relOfPair_unique` | 116-119 | Uniqueness: any relation containing `(v, w)` is `relOfPair v w`. | вАФ |
| `rel_iff_relOfPair` | 121-124 | Characterisation: `rel i v w = true вЖФ i = relOfPair v w`. | вАФ |
| `relOfPair_symm` | 126-131 | `relOfPair v w = relOfPair w v`. | вАФ |
| `relOfPair_eq_zero_iff` | 139-147 | Diagonal characterisation: `relOfPair v w = 0 вЖФ v = w`. | вАФ |
| `AssociationScheme.ClosedSubset` | 161-166 | **(EOL scheme leg) Closed relation subset = block system.** `I` contains the diagonal `R_0` and is closed under the complex product (`R_i,R_j вИИ I` and `intersectionNumber i j k вЙ† 0` вЯє `R_k вИИ I`). The association-scheme form of a block system / sub-equivalence; on a schurian scheme graph it is a union of scheme relations, hence refinement-visible. | Definition |
| `AssociationScheme.schemeEquiv` | 168-171 | **(EOL scheme leg) The equivalence induced by a relation subset:** `v ~ w` iff `relOfPair v w вИИ I`. Under `ClosedSubset` it is a genuine equivalence (the block system). | Definition |
| `AssociationScheme.schemeEquiv_trans` | 181-198 | **Transitivity from closure under the complex product.** `w` witnesses `intersectionNumber (relOfPair v w)(relOfPair w x)(relOfPair v x) вЙ† 0`, so the `ClosedSubset` closure clause forces `relOfPair v x вИИ I`. Where the scheme's intersection numbers do the work a raw partition could not. | вАФ |
| `AssociationScheme.closedSubset_univ` | 205-207 | The whole relation set is always closed (the trivial "one block" system). | вАФ |
| `AssociationScheme.IsPrimitive` | 209-214 | **(EOL scheme leg) Scheme primitivity:** the only closed subsets are the diagonal `{R_0}` and the whole relation set вАФ no non-trivial block system. The Cameron-free, scheme-theoretic primitivity for the Exhaustive-Obstruction Lemma's leg C on coherent-configuration residuals. | Definition |
| `AssociationScheme.exists_nontrivial_closedSubset_of_not_isPrimitive` | 216-225 | **(Imprimitive вЯє non-trivial block system)** Unfolding `¬ђIsPrimitive`: there is a closed subset `I` neither `{R_0}` nor `univ` вАФ a genuine non-trivial block system. The entry point letting the Route B imprimitive discharge construct its partition `ќ≤` (the `schemeEquiv I` block-class) from the descent's combinatorial `¬ђIsPrimitive` observation. Via `push Not`. | вАФ |
| `AssociationScheme.schemeEquiv_class_eq_iff` | 227-245 | **(Block-class equality characterization)** `{y | schemeEquiv I u y} = {y | schemeEquiv I w y} вЖФ schemeEquiv I u w` for a closed subset `I` вАФ the `schemeEquiv I`-classes are the blocks, equal iff their basepoints are related. The honest characterization of the Route B partition `ќ≤ v := {y | schemeEquiv I v y}`, needed wherever `ќ≤ u = ќ≤ w` must be related back to the scheme (e.g. a future non-recovering `hfiber`). Standard equivalence-class machinery on `schemeEquiv_equivalence`. | вАФ |
| `AssociationScheme.exists_composable_of_intersectionNumber` | 247-265 | **(Phase 2, M1.1c вАФ general)** A nonzero intersection number is realized by a composable triple: `R_k` nonempty вИІ `intersectionNumber i j k вЙ† 0 вЯє вИГ x y z, (x,y) вИИ R_i вИІ (y,z) вИИ R_j вИІ (x,z) вИИ R_k`. The general ingredient the `ClosedSubset`-closure clause needs (reusable for the ¬І5.3 general crux: "the difference of a composite relation is the sum of the parts'"). `R_k`-nonemptiness explicit (the axioms do not force every index inhabited). | вАФ |

## ChainDescent/CascadeOracle.lean

The a-priori cascade-oracle Lean contract (plan: `docs/Archive/ChainDescent/chain-descent-cascade-oracle-lean-brief.md`). Builds axiom-clean (only `refineStep`/`refineStep_iff` + Lean foundationals), no `sorry`. Phase A = soundness/validity, Phase B = the completeness reduction (wired to the axiom-free orbit-recovery theorems), Phase C = the residual obligations: verdict iso-invariance is *discharged conditionally* (`verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete` вАФ it reduces to localisation), and localisation is *split* into (1a) bounded-depth recoverability вАФ **proved** on the cascade class (`RecoverableByDepth` + `recoverableByDepth_cfi`/`_scheme`, anchored by `cellsAreOrbits_of_discrete`) вАФ and (1b) intermediate-to-deep bridging, **open but not GI вИИ P** (cascade-class construction correctness). Only general-class completeness is the GI вИИ P obligation. ¬ІC.0 also proves the deferred-decisions foundation `real_stays_real`.

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `mono` | 59-68 | ¬ІC.0 Orbit monotonicity: an `Aut_{S'}`-orbit pair stays an orbit pair at every smaller individualized set `S вКЖ S'`, so a certified merge can be reused at shallower nodes. | вАФ |
| `real_stays_real` | 70-78 | ¬ІC.0 Deferred-decisions foundation: a genuine decision (no orbit relation) at `S` is still genuine at every larger `S' вКЗ S`, so deferring a real decision never loses it. | вАФ |

Generalizes `recoverableByDepth_scheme` (rank-2 only) to every P-polynomial schurian scheme graph вАФ cycles, Johnson, Hamming, all DRGs вАФ in one oracle-vocabulary export; depth-1 cells non-singleton (genuine recovery at the structural oracle's node). | вАФ |
| `recoverableByDepth_univ` | 857-864 | Every graph is trivially recoverable by depth `n` (individualize everything), so only the *polynomial* depth bound is cascade-class content. | вАФ |
| `CascadeComplete` | 871-878 | Completeness contract: the oracle certifies every genuine `Aut_D`-orbit pair; with soundness it then computes the orbit relation exactly. | Definition |
| `certifies_iff_orbit` | 880-894 | For a sound and complete cascade oracle, it returns `some` exactly on the pairs sharing an `Aut_D`-orbit. | вАФ |
| `CellComplete` | 896-903 | The polynomial completeness contract: the oracle certifies every pair sharing a 1-WL cell (refinement-decidable). | Definition |
| `complete_of_cellComplete_recoverable` | 905-918 | **Key theorem.** At an orbit-recoverable node, certifying every same-cell pair already certifies every orbit вАФ reducing orbit-completeness to a polynomial check. | вАФ |
| `VerdictIsoInvariant` | 965-978 | Iso-invariance contract (strategy ¬І15 gap 2): the oracle's verdict depends only on the iso-invariant 1-WL partition. Derivable вАФ see `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete`. | Definition |
| `cascadeComplete_of_localization` | 980-991 | Capstone: cell-completeness plus all-nodes recoverability yields `CascadeComplete`, naming the open localisation obligation as its hypotheses. | вАФ |
| `cascadeComplete_of_cellsAreOrbits` | 993-1004 | Capstone stated against the single open implication: cell-completeness plus `CellsAreOrbits` at every node yields `CascadeComplete`. | вАФ |
| `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete` | 1006-1021 | **Key theorem.** A sound, complete oracle at orbit-recoverable nodes is automatically iso-invariant, so iso-invariance is part of localisation rather than a separate obligation. | вАФ |
| `computes_orbits_of_complete` | 1023-1035 | Capstone: a sound and complete cascade oracle computes the `Aut_D`-orbit relation exactly (program-level correctness, given the completeness obligation). | вАФ |

| `rankPerm_inv_mul_eq_of_match` | 1052-1064 | ¬ІC.4 M-B вАФ the rank-composition identity behind `colourMatchPerm = g`: if `g` value-matches the two colourings (`ѕЗвВВ вИШ g = ѕЗвВБ`), then `(rankPerm ѕЗвВВ)вБї¬є * rankPerm ѕЗвВБ = g`. Pure `vertexRank_comp` reindexing, no graph structure. | вАФ |
| `colourMatchPerm` | 1066-1076 | ¬ІC.4 **M-B вАФ the colour-match permutation.** The explicit `Equiv.Perm` from the two *discrete* branch colourings, as the rank composition `(rankPerm ѕЗ_w)вБї¬є * (rankPerm ѕЗ_v)` (`ѕЗ_r = warmRefine adj P (indivWithRep n D r)`). Always well-defined given discreteness; `= g` at a recoverable node. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `colourMatchPerm_eq_of_orbit` | 1078-1091 | ¬ІC.4 **M-B completeness linchpin.** An `Aut_D` witness `g` (`g v = w`, `w вИЙ D`) value-matches the two branch colourings (`colourMatch_complete`), so `colourMatchPerm = g` вАФ built from the colours, not assumed. | вАФ |
| `matchOracle` | 1092-1110 | ¬ІC.4 **M-B вАФ the colour-match cascade oracle.** Constructs `colourMatchPerm` (when both footprints discrete) and returns it **iff** it verifies as an `Aut_D` orbit map (`IsAut вИІ P-preserving вИІ fixes D вИІ v вЖ¶ w`). Construct-and-check, not the existential shortcut. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `matchOracle_orbitMapSpec` | 1135-1145 | ¬ІC.4 **M-B soundness вАФ `OrbitMapSpec`, unconditional.** When `matchOracle` fires, its four checks *are* the `OrbitPartition` witness conditions, so the returned perm certifies a genuine `Aut_D` orbit pair. No discreteness/recoverability hypothesis. | вАФ |
| `matchOracle_cellComplete` | 1147-1183 | ¬ІC.4 **M-B completeness вАФ `CellComplete`.** Conditional on every node one-step-discretizing (`hdisc`, = the exposure-depth witness / M-C / "B's core") and `CellsAreOrbits` everywhere (`hco`, = localisation): at a same-cell pair the orbit automorphism exists, `colourMatchPerm = g`, so the oracle fires. | вАФ |
| `matchOracle_cascadeComplete` | 1185-1196 | ¬ІC.4 **M-B capstone вАФ `CascadeComplete`.** `matchOracle` computes the orbit relation exactly, reduced to the two named-open hypotheses (discretizing depth + `CellsAreOrbits`); soundness is already unconditional. | вАФ |
| `matchOracle_verdictIsoInvariant` | 1198-1212 | ¬ІC.4 **M-B вАФ flag iso-invariance, free.** With soundness + completeness, `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete` gives the verdict as a function of the iso-invariant 1-WL partition (strategy ¬І15 gap 2) for `matchOracle` on the recoverable class. | вАФ |
| `discrete_of_samePartition` | 1231-1234 | ¬ІC.4b Discreteness transfers across `samePartition`: `samePartition ѕЗвВБ ѕЗвВВ вЖТ Discrete ѕЗвВБ вЖТ Discrete ѕЗвВВ`. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_samePartition` | 1236-1241 | ¬ІC.4b `warmRefine` respects `samePartition` (specialization of `warmRefine_agree_off'`, `D = вИЕ`): equal-partition starts warm-refine to equal-partition results. | вАФ |
| `samePartition_indivWithRep_insert` | 1243-1284 | ¬ІC.4b **Single-rep footprint = indexed `insert`.** For `r вИЙ D`, `indivWithRep n D r` and `individualizedColouring n (insert r D)` induce the same partition (`r` globally unique either way). | вАФ |
| `discrete_indivWithRep_of_discrete_insert` | 1286-1295 | ¬ІC.4b **The M-B depth-witness bridge.** M-B's `hdisc` follows from discreteness of the *indexed* `individualizedColouring (insert r D)` вАФ connecting the depth witness to the `RecoverableByDepth` framework, class-agnostically. | вАФ |
| `indivWithSet` | 1312-1317 | ¬ІC.5 **M-C вАФ multi-step uniform individualization.** Individualize the committed set `S` by index, plus an explored *set* `R` with a single uniform fresh colour `n+1`. Generalizes `indivWithRep` (`R = {r}`); uniform on `R` is forced by transport (an orbit aut moves `R`). | Definition |
| `indivWithRep_eq_indivWithSet` | 1319-1322 | ¬ІC.5 `indivWithRep n S r = indivWithSet n S {r}` вАФ the singleton bridge to M-B. | вАФ |
| `indivWithSet_transport` | 1324-1343 | ¬ІC.5 **M-C transport.** An orbit aut `g` fixing `S` with `RвВВ = RвВБ.image g` carries the branch-`RвВБ` colouring onto branch-`RвВВ` (`ѕЗвВВ вИШ g = ѕЗвВБ`); the `indivWithRep_transport` generalization (uniform colour on the moved set is what makes it hold). | вАФ |
| `IsColourMatchSet` | 1345-1349 | ¬ІC.5 The multi-step colour-match relation: `t` matches branch-`RвВВ`'s refined colours to branch-`RвВБ`'s. The `IsColourMatch` generalization. | Definition |
| `colourMatchSet_complete` | 1351-1358 | ¬ІC.5 **M-C completeness brick.** The orbit aut `g` (fixing `S`, `RвВВ = RвВБ.image g`) *is* a colour-match (`warmRefine_transport вИШ indivWithSet_transport`). | вАФ |
| `colourMatchSet_unique` | 1360-1370 | ¬ІC.5 **M-C uniqueness brick.** At a discrete branch-`RвВВ` footprint any colour-match `= g`, via the colouring-generic `colourMatch_eq_aut`. | вАФ |
| `harvestSet_isAut_of_discrete` | 1372-1382 | ¬ІC.5 **M-C harvest brick.** At a discrete branch-`RвВВ` footprint the colour-match candidate verifies (`= g`) вАФ the harvest now fires at a footprint discretized by an explored *set* (a sequence), not just one rep. | вАФ |
| `colourMatchPermSet` | 1384-1391 | ¬ІC.5 **M-C вАФ the multi-step colour-match permutation.** The rank composition `(rankPerm ѕЗ_{RвВВ})вБї¬є * (rankPerm ѕЗ_{RвВБ})` for set footprints; `colourMatchPerm` is the `RвВБ={v}, RвВВ={w}` case. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `colourMatchPermSet_eq_of_orbit` | 1393-1403 | ¬ІC.5 `colourMatchPermSet = g` at a recoverable set-footprint (`rankPerm_inv_mul_eq_of_match` вЖР `vertexRank_comp` + `colourMatchSet_complete`); the multi-step `colourMatchPerm_eq_of_orbit`. | вАФ |
| `colourMatchSet_exists_of_cellsAreOrbits` | 1405-1418 | ¬ІC.5 **The multi-step firing certificate exists.** From `CellsAreOrbits` at a same-cell pair, for *any* exploration set `RвВБ` the orbit aut `g`, partner `RвВВ = RвВБ.image g`, and the colour-match all exist. The open piece (M-D) is that the oracle's branch-`w` set *is* `RвВБ.image g` (lockstep). | вАФ |
| `matchOracleSet` | 1431-1451 | ¬ІC.6 **M-D вАФ the multi-step colour-match oracle.** Like `matchOracle` but individualizes a whole explored *set* `expand chain r` (per an exploration selector) on top of the committed path; constructs `colourMatchPermSet`, returns it **iff** it verifies `IsAut вИІ P-preserving вИІ fixes D вИІ v вЖ¶ w`. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `matchOracleSet_orbitMapSpec` | 1480-1490 | ¬ІC.6 **M-D soundness вАФ `OrbitMapSpec`, unconditional.** When it fires the four checks *are* the `OrbitPartition` witness; no discreteness/recoverability/lockstep hypothesis. | вАФ |
| `LockstepExpand` | 1492-1502 | ¬ІC.6 **The lockstep correspondence** as equivariance of the exploration rule: any `P`-preserving automorphism fixing the committed path carries one branch's exploration set onto the other's (`expand chain (g v) = (expand chain v).image g`). Discharged for `forcedExpand` (`Cascade.lean`). | Definition |
| `matchOracleSet_cellComplete` | 1504-1544 | ¬ІC.6 **M-D completeness вАФ `CellComplete`.** Reduced to set-footprint discreteness (the multi-step depth witness) + `CellsAreOrbits` + `LockstepExpand`: the lockstep supplies `RвВВ = RвВБ.image g`, so `colourMatchPermSet = g` and the oracle fires. | вАФ |
| `matchOracleSet_cascadeComplete` | 1546-1558 | ¬ІC.6 **M-D capstone вАФ `CascadeComplete`** (the multi-step oracle computes the orbit relation exactly), reduced to the three named-open hypotheses. | вАФ |
| `matchOracleSet_verdictIsoInvariant` | 1560-1573 | ¬ІC.6 **M-D вАФ flag iso-invariance, free** (via `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete`). | вАФ |
| `matchOracle_fires_of_insertDiscrete` | 1606-1629 | ¬ІC.7 **Honest per-node firing (`hco`-free).** At a node where committing the path plus the query rep discretizes (the indexed `RecoverableByDepth` form, bridged by ¬ІC.4b), `matchOracle` fires on **any** genuine `Aut_D` orbit pair `(v,w)` (`v,w вИЙ D`) вАФ the orbit witness is consumed directly, so no `CellsAreOrbits`. | вАФ |
| `matchOracle_orbit_of_fire_mono` | 1631-1645 | ¬ІC.7 **Propagate via `mono`.** A merge certified at a node holds at every shallower committed set `S вКЖ chain.D` (`OrbitPartition.mono`) вАФ the "fire deep, prune shallow" step. | вАФ |
| `matchOracle_certifies_iff_orbit_of_insertDiscrete` | 1647-1673 | ¬ІC.7 **Exact orbit decider at the discretizing depth.** At a footprint-discretizing node, `matchOracle` fires on `(v,w)` **iff** they are a genuine `Aut_D` orbit pair (`hco`-free). Limits: holds only under the discreteness hypotheses (cascade depth), and decides the *path-fixing* `Aut_D`, not global `Aut`. | вАФ |
| `indivWithSeq` | 1694-1699 | ¬ІC.8 **Level-coloured exploration sequence (Leg 1).** Committed `S` by index plus the `i`-th element of `rs` by its *position* colour `n+1+i`; the position colouring (not vertex index) is what transports under an orbit automorphism. | Definition |
| `samePartition_indivWithSeq` | 1710-1778 | ¬ІC.8 **A1: level-coloured sequence = indexed union.** `indivWithSeq n S rs` and the indexed `individualizedColouring n (S вИ™ rs.toFinset)` induce the same partition (each `rs`-vertex globally unique); unconditional. | вАФ |
| `discrete_indivWithSeq_of_discrete_union` | 1780-1791 | ¬ІC.8 **The Leg-1 depth-witness bridge (sequence).** Sequence-footprint discreteness follows from discreteness of the indexed `individualizedColouring n (S вИ™ rs.toFinset)`, so `hdiscSeq вЯЄ recoverableByDepth`. Sequence generalization of `discrete_indivWithRep_of_discrete_insert`. | вАФ |
| `idxOf_map_of_injective` | 1805-1817 | ¬ІC.8 **Position preserved by `map`.** `(l.map g).idxOf (g a) = l.idxOf a` for a permutation `g` вАФ the pure-list core of sequence transport. | вАФ |
| `indivWithSeq_transport` | 1819-1840 | ¬ІC.8 **A2 transport.** An orbit aut `g` fixing `S` with `rsвВВ = rsвВБ.map g` carries the branch-`rsвВБ` level colouring onto branch-`rsвВВ` (`ѕЗвВВ вИШ g = ѕЗвВБ`) вАФ position via `idxOf_map_of_injective`, off-sequence via `individualizedColouring` invariance. | вАФ |
| `IsColourMatchSeq` | 1842-1845 | ¬ІC.8 The sequence colour-match relation (`IsColourMatchSet` analogue): `t` matches branch-`rsвВВ`'s refined colours to branch-`rsвВБ`'s. | Definition |
| `colourMatchSeq_complete` | 1847-1854 | ¬ІC.8 **Sequence completeness brick.** The orbit aut `g` (fixing `S`, `rsвВВ = rsвВБ.map g`) *is* a colour-match (`warmRefine_transport вИШ indivWithSeq_transport`). | вАФ |
| `colourMatchPermSeq` | 1856-1863 | ¬ІC.8 **The sequence colour-match permutation.** Rank composition `(rankPerm ѕЗ_{rsвВВ})вБї¬є * rankPerm ѕЗ_{rsвВБ}` for level-coloured footprints; `colourMatchPermSet` with the uniform set replaced by the sequence. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `colourMatchSeq_exists_of_cellsAreOrbits` | 1877-1890 | ¬ІC.8 **The level-coloured firing certificate exists.** From `CellsAreOrbits`, for any sequence `rsвВБ` the orbit aut `g`, partner `rsвВВ = rsвВБ.map g`, and the colour-match exist. The open piece is the ordered lockstep (A2b). | вАФ |
| `matchOracleSeq` | 1903-1923 | ¬ІC.8 **The multi-step sequence colour-match oracle.** Like `matchOracleSet` but individualizes the ordered sequence `expand chain r` via `indivWithSeq` (so its depth witness is A1-reducible); construct-and-check on `colourMatchPermSeq`. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `matchOracleSeq_orbitMapSpec` | 1951-1960 | ¬ІC.8 **Sequence soundness вАФ `OrbitMapSpec`, unconditional.** When it fires the four checks *are* the `OrbitPartition` witness. | вАФ |
| `LockstepExpandSeq` | 1962-1973 | ¬ІC.8 **The sequence lockstep.** The ordered (`map`, not `image`) `LockstepExpand` analogue: `expand chain (g v) = (expand chain v).map g`. Strictly stronger than the set lockstep; provably false in the multi-step regime (`lockstep_disc_imp_stab_trivial`). | Definition |
| `matchOracleSeq_cellComplete` | 1975-2014 | ¬ІC.8 **Sequence completeness вАФ `CellComplete`.** Reduced to `hdiscSeq` (A1-reducible) + `hco` + `LockstepExpandSeq`. | вАФ |
| `matchOracleSeq_cascadeComplete` | 2016-2028 | ¬ІC.8 **Sequence capstone вАФ `CascadeComplete`**, reduced to the same three hypotheses (the last jointly unsatisfiable with `hdiscSeq` for multi-step вАФ see `lockstep_disc_imp_stab_trivial`). | вАФ |
| `matchOracleSeq_verdictIsoInvariant` | 2030-2043 | ¬ІC.8 **Sequence flag iso-invariance, free** (via `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete`). | вАФ |
| `lockstep_disc_imp_stab_trivial` | 2075-2109 | ¬ІC.8 **The discretizing-oracle limit (conservation of obstruction).** `LockstepExpandSeq вИІ hdiscSeq вЯє stab_{Aut_D}(v) = 1`: the sequence oracle's completeness hypotheses hold jointly only in the single-rep regime, so the discretizing colour-match cannot harvest a multi-step moved orbit (вЖТ cross-branch / SchreierвАУSims). | вАФ |
## ChainDescent/LinearOracle.lean

The linear-oracle / abelian-stripping work (tractable-buildout B2; plan + status in `docs/chain-descent-linear-oracle.md` ¬І8.2). Built on the ¬І15.8 scaffolding (`DirAssignment`/`flipPair`/`LinearOracleSpec`/`LeafTwistSpec`/`canonAdj`). Builds axiom-clean (`refineStep`/`refineStep_iff` + foundationals), no `sorry`. **B2 soundness core DONE 2026-05-30:** ¬ІL.1 soundness anchor, ¬ІL.2 the *forced* candidate twist (rank rebasing вАФ the construction is determined, not searched; the `canonAdj_rebase` bridge), ¬ІL.3 abelian `ZвВВ^d` structure. Remaining: `canonForm` lex-min tie (needs descent-with-pruning model), completeness, lifting twists to subgroup `N` (Part A).

### ¬ІL.1 вАФ Soundness anchor (B2.1)

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `RealizesFlip` | 52-61 | **Soundness anchor.** The relation "twist `t` relabels branch `ѕГ`'s leaf to the flipped branch `flipPair ѕГ a b`'s leaf" вАФ the `LeafTwistSpec` conclusion with the partner branch pinned to the flip, i.e. the pruning justification. | Definition |
| `TwistWitness` | 63-83 | The verified data a twist discovery returns: the decided pair `(a,b)`, the candidate permutation `t`, its `IsAut` proof (the ¬І4.5 edge-check, sole soundness anchor), and a `RealizesFlip` proof. | Structure |
| `twistOracle` | 85-95 | A concrete `LinearOracleSpec` parameterised by an abstracted `discover` function (C#-side canonical-id matching); returns the verified automorphism from a `TwistWitness`, `none` otherwise. Verification lives inside the witness, so every output is a genuine automorphism. | Definition |
| `twistOracle_leafTwist` | 97-116 | **Key theorem (B2.1 discharge).** `twistOracle` satisfies `LeafTwistSpec`, with the flipped branch as the explicit witness `ѕГ' = flipPair ѕГ` (sharper than the bare existential) вАФ closing the pruning-justification contract for any sound discovery. | вАФ |

### ¬ІL.2 вАФ The forced candidate twist (B2.2 + most of B2.3)

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `canonAdj_rebase` | 159-174 | **The rebasing bridge.** Relabelling `ѕГ`'s canonical leaf by the rank rebasing `rankPerm ѕА_{ѕГ'} * (rankPerm ѕА_ѕГ)вБї¬є` yields `ѕГ'`'s leaf; the flip is the `ѕГ' = flipPair ѕГ` instance. | вАФ |
| `candidateTwist` | 184-192 | **The forced candidate twist** for decision `(a,b)`: the rank rebasing `rankPerm ѕА_flip * (rankPerm ѕА_ѕГ)вБї¬є`. Always realises the flip; the twist is determined, not searched. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `candidateTwist_realizesFlip` | 194-201 | The forced candidate always realises the flip вАФ the construction is forced, with no ambiguity. | вАФ |
| `candidateTwist_unique` | 203-215 | **Determinacy.** The candidate is the unique permutation rank-aligning `ѕГ` to the flipped branch вАФ the leaf-level iso-invariance gate, making twist discovery deterministic in iso-invariant rank data. | вАФ |
| `twistWitness_of_isAut` | 217-234 | The oracle reduces to one check: a verified-automorphism forced candidate yields a complete `TwistWitness`. Discovery is a single decidable edge-check. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `canonicalTwistOracle` | 235-249 | **The canonical twist oracle.** A fully concrete `LinearOracleSpec`: for the selected pair, compute the forced candidate and return it iff it verifies as an automorphism. The only abstracted piece is pair selection (soundness-irrelevant). | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `canonicalTwistOracle_leafTwist` | 251-259 | **Key theorem.** `canonicalTwistOracle` satisfies `LeafTwistSpec` (it is a `twistOracle`) вАФ a concrete verified linear oracle, sound by construction. | вАФ |

### ¬ІL.3 вАФ Abelian structure (B2.4, partial)

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `candidateTwist_flip_inv` | 282-291 | **`ZвВВ` involution.** The forced candidate for the flip-back is the inverse of the candidate for the flip; with `flipPair_comm` this is the elementary-abelian `ZвВВ^d` structure of the residual. | вАФ |

### ¬ІL.4 вАФ Completeness / effectiveness (when the oracle fires)

Characterizes *when* the oracle fires and proves firing is semantically justified. The
oracle is complete exactly on the **abelian regime** (forced candidate вИИ Aut) вАФ the
calculator ¬І6 boundary; the general converse fails (conjugation gap). The
abelian-sufficiency lemma (forced candidate IsAut for genuine abelian flips, via
`warm_6_2` rank machinery) is the open core scoped in the ¬ІL.4 doc-comment.

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `isAut_candidateTwist_iff_aligned` | 329-344 | **Firing characterisation.** The forced candidate is an automorphism iff some automorphism is rank-aligned (`g ¬Ј ѕА_ѕГ = ѕА_flip`) вАФ so the whole completeness question is "does a rank-aligned automorphism exist?" | вАФ |
| `RealizableFlip` | 346-352 | The decision is a genuine `Aut(adj)` symmetry: some automorphism realises the flip (the two branches are isomorphic) вАФ what pruning should require. | Definition |
| `realizableFlip_of_isAut_candidateTwist` | 354-365 | **Firing is semantically justified.** When the forced candidate verifies, the branches are genuinely `Aut(adj)`-equivalent (the candidate is the witness) вАФ pruning reflects a real symmetry. | вАФ |
| `canonicalTwistOracle_isSome_iff` | 367-383 | **Key theorem.** Given the pair selector returns `(a,b)`, the oracle fires iff the forced candidate is an automorphism вАФ the entire completeness question is one decidable edge-check. | вАФ |
| `candidateTwist_flipBack_isAut` | 385-396 | **`ZвВВ`-direction consistency.** If the forced candidate for `ѕГ вЖТ flip` verifies, so does the candidate for the flip-back вАФ the oracle prunes both directions of a genuine `ZвВВ` decision consistently. | вАФ |

### ¬ІL.5 вАФ Toward abelian sufficiency (partial)

The open core of completeness вАФ *forced candidate вИИ Aut for abelian decisions* вАФ needs
gadget-level rank-alignment (at a leaf both branches are discrete, so `warm_6_2`'s
partition equality is vacuous; the content is in the rank order). Provable progress:

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `candidateTwist_eq_one_of_rankPerm_eq` | 424-435 | **Absorbed decision.** Equal leaf rank permutations force the candidate to be the identity вАФ the degenerate end of the abelian regime. | вАФ |

### ¬ІL.7 вАФ The CFI bridge (M1b): candidate as a conjugate of a graph automorphism

Now that `refineStep` is concrete, the cross-config transport (`¬І16.2b` in ChainDescent.lean)
lets us express the forced candidate via a *real* automorphism. A **config-swap** `g` carries the
ѕГ-branch config onto the flip-branch config; it forces `ѕА_ѕГ = ѕА_flip ¬Ј g`, so the candidate is the
`ѕА_ѕГ`-conjugate of `gвБї¬є`. This reduces the opaque `IsAut candidate adj` to the structural gadget
rank-alignment, isolating the genuine CFI nut (shared with Tier-3a B1 `hwit`): (1) a config-swap
exists, (2) its `ѕА_ѕГ`-conjugate is an automorphism.

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `ConfigSwap` | 587-599 | A config-swap for decision `(a,b)`: a graph automorphism carrying the ѕГ-branch configuration onto the flip-branch configuration (fixes `ѕЗќє`, sends `ѕГ.ѕГ` to `(flipPair ѕГ).ѕГ`). For CFI, the gadget twist swapping the decided pair. | Structure |
| `configSwap_rankPerm` / `_flip` | The leaf rank perms differ by `g`: `ѕА_ѕГ = ѕА_flip ¬Ј g` (resp. `ѕА_flip = ѕА_ѕГ ¬Ј gвБї¬є`), from transport + `vertexRank_comp`. | axiom-light |
| `candidateTwist_eq_conjugate` | 627-637 | **The rank-space reduction.** Given a config-swap `g`, the forced candidate is the `ѕА_ѕГ`-conjugate of `gвБї¬є` (`candidateTwist = ѕА_ѕГ ¬Ј gвБї¬є ¬Ј ѕА_ѕГвБї¬є`) вАФ the opaque rebasing exposed as a conjugate of a genuine automorphism. | вАФ |
| `isAut_candidateTwist_iff_conjugate` | 639-650 | **The reduction.** `IsAut candidate adj вЖФ IsAut (ѕА_ѕГ ¬Ј gвБї¬є ¬Ј ѕА_ѕГвБї¬є) adj` вАФ the rank-space firing obligation is exactly the gadget rank-alignment, the concrete nut shared with Tier-3a B1. | вАФ |

**¬ІL.7b вАФ vertex-model soundness (Approach C, the faithful C# model).** A config-swap is a real
graph automorphism, so both branches give the *same canonical leaf* вАФ no rank-alignment needed. This
is the soundness the C# `TwistConstruction` actually uses (it verifies a vertex automorphism, not the
rank rebasing).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `canonAdj_eq_of_configSwap` | 661-676 | **Equal canonical leaves.** A config-swap implies both branches produce the identical canonical leaf вАФ the vertex-model soundness statement (pruning the flip branch loses nothing), needing no rank-alignment. | вАФ |
| `realizableFlip_of_configSwap` | 678-692 | A config-swap implies `RealizableFlip` (identity witness, since the leaves coincide) вАФ the decision is a genuine `Aut(adj)` symmetry with no rank-alignment obligation. | вАФ |

**¬ІL.8 вАФ CFI completeness: config-swap from a swapping automorphism (M1c step 3, the cascade-1b bridge).**
*Where a config-swap comes from.* A swapping automorphism `g` (`g a = b`, `g b = a`) is exactly an
`OrbitPartition adj P S a b` witness specialised to the size-2 decision cell вАФ the cascade oracle's
currency. So linear-oracle CFI completeness reduces to the **shared cascade-1b** obligation
(bounded-depth half `recoverableByDepth_cfi` proved; decision-node-depth bridge open, *not* `GIвИИP`).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `configSwap_of_aut` | 724-767 | **General constructor (the `hwit` entry point).** *Any* swapping automorphism `g` (`g a = b`, `g b = a`) that fixes `ѕЗќє` and preserves `ѕГ.ѕГ` *off the flip pair* (`ѕГ.ѕГ (g v)(g u) = ѕГ.ѕГ v u` for `(v,u) вИЙ {(a,b),(b,a)}`) is a `ConfigSwap` вАФ `g` need **not** be a transposition (may move the whole coupled component). Removes the config-swap *packaging* from the open content: once the CFI gadget twist `g` and its off-pair `ѕГ`-action are known, the `ConfigSwap` is built with no rank-alignment. | Definition |
| `configSwap_of_swap` | 769-820 | **Closed instance (the `ZвВВ` twin-swap).** A ѕГ-cell-coherent transposition automorphism (`g` swaps `a,b`, fixes the rest and `ѕЗќє`) is a `ConfigSwap` вАФ the simplest genuine abelian decision. Now a thin specialisation of `configSwap_of_aut` (transposition вЗТ off-pair preservation = ѕГ-cell-coherence). | Definition |
| `configSwap_of_twin` | 822-850 | **The twin вЖТ config-swap bridge.** An (adj, ѕГ)-twin decision pair (adjacency-twin on a simple graph plus ѕГ-cell-coherent, `ѕЗќє a = ѕЗќє b`) admits a `ConfigSwap` via the transposition `(a b)` вАФ the linear-oracle analog of `cellsAreOrbits_of_twin_cells`, both oracles firing on the same twin/module class through one shared lemma. Not CFI (which has no twins). | Definition |
| `ConfigSwapRecoverable` | 852-862 | **Decision-node recoverability** (the named cascade-1b obligation for the linear oracle): every leaf decision admits a config-swap. The graph-level analog of `AbelianSufficiencyHolds`; open discharge `configSwapRecoverable_of_cfi` is downstream. | Definition |
| `canonAdj_eq_of_configSwapRecoverable` | 864-875 | **Capstone (pruning soundness).** Config-swap-recoverability implies both branches give the identical canonical leaf at every decision вАФ reducing the oracle's effectiveness to the single `ConfigSwapRecoverable` hypothesis. | вАФ |
| `realizableFlip_of_configSwapRecoverable` | 877-888 | **Capstone (real symmetry).** Config-swap-recoverability implies every leaf decision is a genuine `Aut(adj)` symmetry вАФ vertex-model completeness, no rank-alignment needed. | вАФ |

**¬ІL.9 вАФ CFI gadget twist fires the oracle (Phase 6a: wiring the Stage-3 cycle-space flip).** The
Stage-3 gadget flip (`CFI.lean ¬І15`, `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut`) is now constructed; this section wires it into
`configSwap_of_aut` and reduces `ConfigSwapRecoverable` for CFI to the existence of the right cycle `F`
per decision.

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `configSwap_of_cfiFlipAut` | **The CFI gadget twist is a config-swap** (unconditional bridge). `configSwap_of_aut` instantiated with `g := cfiFlipAut F` (an `Aut(adj)` involution by `isAut_cfiFlipAut`): if the flip swaps `(a,b)`, fixes `ѕЗќє`, and carries `ѕГ` off the pair, it is a `ConfigSwap`. The concrete soundness вАФ the vertex-space gadget twist (the C#'s witness) fires the oracle, no rank-alignment. | Definition |
| `CFIGadgetFlippable` | **The named cascade-1b residual.** Every leaf decision admits an even-symmetric cycle `F` whose gadget flip swaps `(a,b)`, fixes `ѕЗќє`, carries `ѕГ` off the pair. Commits the CFI witness to the gadget-flip mechanism (matching the C#); the open content is purely `F`'s existence per decision (cascade-1b). | Definition |
| `configSwapRecoverable_of_cfi` | **`ConfigSwapRecoverable` for CFI via the gadget flip.** `CFIGadgetFlippable h вЖТ ConfigSwapRecoverable` вАФ the discharge reduced to its irreducible combinatorial core (the decision-local even cycle's existence). Feeds the capstones вЯє oracle fires on every CFI decision. | вАФ |

Open (not a `sorry`): **`CFIGadgetFlippable`** вАФ that the decision-local even cycle `F` *exists* for every
decision (the flip is built and proven sound; what remains is the cycle through the decision edge, local
to the decided gadget). Its three per-decision obligations (swap `(a,b)`, fix `ѕЗќє`, carry `ѕГ` off the
pair) are the descent-coherence content of cascade-1b вАФ the decision-node-depth half, shared with the
cascade oracle, *not* `GIвИИP`.

**¬ІL.9 follow-on вАФ the conditions reduced to locality + cell-coherence.** Decouples the gadget-flip
mechanics from the descent's cell structure, so the residual is the cascade-1b shape (F-locality +
cell-coherence), not the opaque `configSwap_of_aut` package.

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `swapsConfig_off_pair_of_local` | **The ѕГ-off-pair reduction (general `g`, reusable).** Any `g` swapping `(a,b)`, fixing decided vertices off `{a,b}`, preserving the decided set and `PвВА`, satisfies the off-pair condition given only **ѕГ-cell-coherence** at `(a,b)`. Off-D via `agrees_off` + PвВА-invariance; on-D via the coherence case-analysis. | вАФ |
| `preserves_D_of_involutive_local` | Decided-set preservation for an involutive local swap (`g x вИИ D вЖФ x вИИ D` from `g¬≤=id` + swap + fix-off-`{a,b}`). The `hgD` input above, discharged for the gadget flip. | вАФ |
| `cfiFlipAut_fixesѕЗќє_of_support` | **The `hgѕЗ` reduction.** The flip fixes `ѕЗќє` once it does on the F-touched gadgets вАФ Phase-4 locality fixes every `F`-free gadget outright. Reduces global `hgѕЗ` to ѕЗќє-coherence on the (small) F-support. | вАФ |
| `configSwap_of_cfiFlipAut_local` | **The reduced bridge.** A `ConfigSwap` from {`F` even+symmetric, swap, **F is D-local**, ѕГ-cell-coherent, `PвВА` Aut-invariant, ѕЗќє-coherent on F-support} вАФ the three `configSwap_of_aut` conditions discharged via the reductions above. | Definition |
| `CFIGadgetFlippableLocal` | The reduced per-decision predicate: an even-symmetric **D-local** `F` whose flip swaps `(a,b)`, with ѕГ cell-coherent and ѕЗќє coherent on the F-support. The conditions are now the descent-coherence / cycle-locality (cascade-1b) facts. | Definition |
| `configSwapRecoverable_of_cfi_local` | `ConfigSwapRecoverable` from `CFIGadgetFlippableLocal` (+ `PвВА` Aut-invariance) вАФ the discharge via the decoupled hypotheses. | вАФ |

**¬ІL.9 (C1b.1) вАФ the CFI glue: parity-pair decisions.** Reduces `CFIGadgetFlippableLocal` to the
explicit-edge form, discharging the swap obligation in advance (via C1b.0).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `CFIParityDecisionFlippable` | The reduced cascade-1b hypothesis: every decision `(a,b)` is the parity-pair of a base edge `{v,w}` (`a = e^{bвВА}_{vвЖТw}`, `b = e^{¬ђbвВА}`) admitting an even-symmetric cycle `F` with `{v,w} вИИ F`, D-local, ѕГ/ѕЗќє cell-coherent. The swap is no longer an obligation (it's `cfiFlipAut_swaps_endpointVertex`); only cycle existence + coherence remain. | Definition |
| `cfiGadgetFlippableLocal_of_parity` | **The C1b.1 glue.** `CFIParityDecisionFlippable вЖТ CFIGadgetFlippableLocal` вАФ the body's two swap conjuncts from `cfiFlipAut_endpointVertex` + `F v w = true`; the rest passes through. Open content narrows to C1b.2 (cycle exists) + C1b.3 (decisions are parity-pairs + coherence). | вАФ |

Transport chain it builds on (ChainDescent.lean `¬І16.2b`): `signature_transport`, `sigKey_transport`,
`refineStep_transport`, `iterate_refineStep_transport`, `warmRefine_transport` вАФ cross-config (two
`(P,ѕЗ)` related by an automorphism), the value-level generalisation of the `*_invariant_of_isAut`
chain, newly provable because `refineStep` is concrete. All axiom-light.

### ¬ІL.6 вАФ Relativized completeness (the retargeting)

The general completeness statement ("forced candidate fires whenever the branches are
isomorphic") *provably* cannot close вАФ a realizing aut agrees with the forced candidate only
up to a conjugate of `Aut(adj)` (`rankPerm_comp`), the split-or-Johnson wall *by design*, and
the **same gap the a-priori cascade oracle carries** (`CascadeOracle.lean` ¬І4.3). The fix is
the cascade oracle's **Phase-B move**: relativize completeness to the recoverable/abelian
class and reduce it to orbit recovery. This scaffold names the relativized target and isolates
the one open obligation (`AbelianSufficiencyHolds` on the CFI class вАФ the leaf-level instance
of orbit recovery, the same nut as Tier-3a B1's `hwit`).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `RankAligned` | 482-490 | The algebraic firing condition: a rank-aligned automorphism exists (`вИГ g вИИ Aut(adj), g ¬Ј ѕА_ѕГ = ѕА_flip`). The oracle fires exactly when this holds. | Definition |
| `isAut_candidateTwist_iff_rankAligned` | 492-500 | **Interface.** The forced candidate is an automorphism iff `RankAligned` вАФ the completeness question restated against the named predicate. | вАФ |
| `AbelianSufficiency` | 502-512 | **The per-decision relativized completeness target.** `RealizableFlip вЖТ IsAut candidate`: if the flip is a real symmetry then the forced candidate verifies. False in the non-abelian regime (the wall); the claim to discharge on the abelian/cascade class. | Definition |
| `oracleFires_of_abelianSufficiency` | 514-529 | **Capstone (what suffices).** `AbelianSufficiency` plus a real symmetry implies the oracle fires вАФ the linear-oracle analog of cascade's `cascadeComplete_of_localization`. | вАФ |
| `abelianSufficiency_of_rankPerm_eq` | 531-542 | **Non-vacuous closed instance.** The absorbed decision is abelian-sufficient (candidate `= 1 вИИ Aut` outright) вАФ validates the scaffold against a real instance. | вАФ |
| `AbelianSufficiencyHolds` | 544-552 | The graph-level discharge target: every leaf decision is abelian-sufficient. Open obligation `abelianSufficiencyHolds_of_cfi` is downstream (via `theorem_1_HOR_cfi_oddDeg`, the same nut as Tier-3a B1's `hwit`). | Definition |
| `oracleFires_of_abelianSufficiencyHolds` | 554-568 | **Graph-level capstone.** `AbelianSufficiencyHolds` implies the oracle fires at every leaf decision that is a real symmetry вАФ relativized completeness on the abelian class. | вАФ |

## ChainDescent/Group.lean

Part A (A1вАУA3) of `docs/chain-descent-tier3-tractable-buildout.md` вАФ the group object
the orbit-recovery program deliberately avoided, now needed for Tier-3 vocabulary
(`HвВА вКµ вА¶ вКµ H_k`, quotient graphs). Pure glue over Mathlib group theory + the existing
`IsAut` lemmas; **no `refineStep`** dependency (axioms `[propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound]`).
A4 (the quotient *graph* `G/H` + cell = quotient-vertex lemma) is **not** here вАФ it is the
medium-risk Mathlib gap gating B1.

### A1 вАФ `Aut(G)` as a group

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `AutGroup adj` | ¬ІA1 **The automorphism group.** `{ѕА | IsAut ѕА adj}` as a `Subgroup (Equiv.Perm (Fin n))` вАФ the group object Tier-3 vocabulary (`HвВА вКµ вА¶ вКµ H_k`, quotient graphs) is stated over. | Definition |
| `mem_autGroup` | 69-70 | Membership in `AutGroup adj` is exactly `IsAut ѕА adj` (`@[simp]` unfolding). | `@[simp]` |
| `orbitPartition_iff_autGroup` | 72-87 | ¬ІA1 **The `OrbitPartition` вЖФ `AutGroup` bridge.** Repackages the bare permutation of the orbit relation as a genuine group element in the pointwise-`S`-stabilizer that preserves `P`, keeping `OrbitPartition` the working object while exposing the group element where the chain needs it. | вАФ |

### A2 вАФ Action on vertices + orbit bridge

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `autGroup_smul` | 96-98 | ¬ІA2 The subgroup action's `smul` is permutation application: `g вАҐ v = (вЖСg) v` (`@[simp]`). | `@[simp]` |
| `mem_orbit_autGroup_iff` | 100-109 | ¬ІA2 **Orbit membership, unfolded.** `w` lies in `v`'s `AutGroup`-orbit iff some automorphism sends `v` to `w` (the pure-orbit form, before `OrbitPartition`'s `P`-preservation refinement). | вАФ |
| `mem_orbit_autGroup_iff_orbitPartition` | 111-125 | ¬ІA2 **The orbit bridge.** Under `P`-invariance, `v`'s `AutGroup`-orbit coincides with the root relation `OrbitPartition adj P вИЕ` вАФ the group-level reading of the support backbone's root case. | вАФ |

| Name | Description | Notes |
