| `LayerChain.trivial` | ¬ІA3 **The trivial chain** `AutGroup adj вКµ вК•` (length 1); witnesses `LayerChain` is inhabited. | Definition |

### A4 вАФ quotient graph + cell = quotient-vertex

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `orbitSetoid adj P S` | ¬ІA4 The `Aut_S`-orbit relation `OrbitPartition adj P S` packaged as a `Setoid` from its proved `refl`/`symm`/`trans`. | Definition |
| `OrbitQuotient adj P S` | ¬ІA4 **The quotient vertex set** `V(G)/Aut_S` вАФ the vertices of the quotient graph. | `abbrev` |
| `orbitMk` / `orbitMk_eq_iff` | The quotient map `v вЖ¶ вЯ¶vвЯІ`; `orbitMk v = orbitMk w вЖФ OrbitPartition adj P S v w`. | Definition / `Quotient.eq` |
| `cell_iff_orbitMk_eq` | 226-242 | ¬ІA4 **The cell = quotient-vertex lemma.** Under `CellsAreOrbits`, two vertices share a 1-WL cell of `(G, S)` iff they are the same quotient vertex вАФ the correspondence B1's cascade-composition induction steps through. | вАФ |
| `QuotientAdjCompatible` | 246-254 | ¬ІA4 **Quotient-adjacency compatibility.** The condition that `adj v w` is constant on `Aut_S`-orbit pairs вАФ exactly when a simple induced adjacency on the quotient is well-defined (holds at discreteness, fails for coarser `S`). | Definition |
| `quotientAdj` / `quotientAdj_mk` | The induced adjacency on `OrbitQuotient`, well-defined under `QuotientAdjCompatible` (via `Quotient.liftвВВ`); `quotientAdj h вЯ¶vвЯІ вЯ¶wвЯІ = adj.adj v w` (`rfl`). | Definition / `@[simp]` |
| `quotientAdjCompatible_of_discrete` | 269-280 | ¬ІA4 At discreteness the quotient graph is always well-defined (orbits are singletons) вАФ the recursion-bottom anchor, paralleling `cellsAreOrbits_of_discrete`. | вАФ |
| `orbitPartition_empty_iff_orbitRel` | 290-302 | ¬ІA4 The root orbit relation `OrbitPartition adj P вИЕ` equals the `AutGroup` `MulAction` orbit relation (under `P`-invariance) вАФ the relational form of the A2 orbit bridge, symmetrised for `orbitRel`. | вАФ |
| `orbitQuotientEquivAutGroup` | 304-312 | ¬ІA4 **The root quotient is `V(G)/Aut(G)`.** Under `P`-invariance, `OrbitQuotient adj P вИЕ` is equivalent to the `MulAction` orbit quotient of `AutGroup adj`, tying A4's relational quotient back to A1/A2's group object. | Definition |

| `stabilizer_eq_bot_of_isPretransitive_comm` | 324-342 | **(seal core L1, [exhaustive-obstruction ¬І0.7](../docs/chain-descent-exhaustive-obstruction.md))** A transitive, faithful, **abelian** action is **free**: every point-stabilizer is trivial ("transitive abelian вЯє regular"). The textbook root of "no non-consumed abelian species". | вАФ |
| `existsUnique_smul_of_isPretransitive_comm` | 344-355 | **(seal core L2)** Unique candidate: in a transitive faithful abelian action exactly one group element moves `a` to `b` (existence from transitivity, uniqueness from L1's trivial stabilizer). | вАФ |
| `smul_eq_on_orbit_of_comm` | 357-366 | **(seal core L3 вАФ load-bearing, axiom-free)** Quotient-free, faithfulness-free form: if `g, h` both move `a` to `b` then they agree on the **whole orbit** of `a` (`gвАҐc = kвАҐb = hвАҐc` for `c = kвАҐa`). The "unique-candidate-on-the-cell" the linear-oracle harvest reads вАФ holds for an abelian residual even with non-trivial global stabilizers (CFI). | вАФ |
| `aut_agree_on_orbit_of_comm` | 368-382 | **(seal instantiation)** L3 for `AutGroup adj`: an **abelian residual** вЯє two automorphisms both sending `a вЖ¶ b` agree on every `c` in `a`'s orbit, so the decision is determined on its cell (always consumable). | вАФ |
| `not_comm_of_orbit_disagree` | 384-393 | **(seal headline вАФ no non-consumed abelian species)** Contrapositive: a decision `a вЖ¶ b` whose two candidate automorphisms **disagree** on the cell forces a **non-abelian** residual. With the ¬І12 capstone (large primitive non-abelian вЯє Cameron), the only non-consumed symmetry is a Cameron section вАФ the bottom-up, citation-free half of the seal. | вАФ |
| `card_eq_of_isPretransitive_comm` | 404-418 | **(seal Step 4 вАФ order side, [exhaustive-obstruction ¬І0.7](../docs/chain-descent-exhaustive-obstruction.md))** A transitive, faithful, **abelian** action has `Nat.card G = Nat.card ќ±`: the orbit map `g вЖ¶ gвАҐa` is a bijection (free from L1, surjective from transitivity), so order = degree ("abelian primitive вЯє regular, hence small"). | вАФ |
| `not_comm_of_isPretransitive_of_stabilizer_ne_bot` | 420-426 | **(seal Step 4, qualitative)** A transitive faithful action with a **non-trivial** point stabilizer (not regular) is **non-abelian** вАФ direct contrapositive of L1. | вАФ |
| `not_comm_of_isPreprimitive_card_lt` | 428-437 | **(seal Step 4 вАФ the headline: large primitive вЯє non-abelian)** A **preprimitive** faithful action with `Nat.card ќ± < Nat.card G` (group strictly larger than its degree) is **non-abelian**, since a transitive abelian action has order = degree. The order-side proof that a primitive abelian group is `Z_p` (never large); closes the bottom-up route's Step 4 with no citation. | вАФ |
## ChainDescent/Cascade.lean

> **вШЕ SEAL CAPSTONE MAP** (also at the top of the seal section in `Cascade.lean`). 21 public
> `reachesRigidOrCameron_*` capstones remain here (12 superseded ones were archived to
> `PrivateTheoremIndex.md`). **The one to use: `reachesRigidOrCameron_viaBoundedMinMult`**
> (`CascadeAffine.lean`; seal `modulo {G3 + hSmallAutThin + hcatch + hImprim}`, open content =
> `hSmallAutThin` = node 4). Other LIVE endpoints: `вА¶_viaNoCover` (poly node-4 anchor),
> `вА¶_viaSmallAutShatters` (sub-exp citation), `вА¶_viaG0powNeg` (closure discharged), `вА¶_affineSlice`
> (cited 2-sep), `вА¶_viaCompleteBase` (node-2 rung). Everything else here is a load-bearing intermediate
> of the live proof chain; the 12 superseded capstones now live (full text) in `PrivateTheoremIndex.md`.

B1 (Tier 3a cascade composition) of `docs/chain-descent-tier3-tractable-buildout.md`,
Phases A + C. Build plan: `docs/chain-descent-tier3a-b1-build-plan.md`. The headline
"depths add" theorem, **conditional on the per-layer transfer** (`LayerStep`, = paper
¬І4.2.5, discharged in the not-yet-built Phase D). Stays on `Fin n` (no quotient
re-typing) by telescoping cumulative individualization sets. Axiom-clean (standard
basis; `refineStep` via `warmRefine`).

### Phase A вАФ interface

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `IsBase adj P T` | **Phase A interface.** `T` is a *base* of the `P`-preserving automorphism group: its pointwise stabilizer is trivial, so the `Aut_T`-orbit relation is equality вАФ the chain's bottom `H_k = {1}`. | Definition |
| `LayerStep adj P T S` | **Phase A interface вАФ the per-layer transfer obligation.** `CellsAreOrbits T вЖТ CellsAreOrbits (T вИ™ S)`: individualizing the increment `S` brings cells down to `Aut_{TвИ™S}`-orbits (paper ¬І4.2.5 transferred to `G`). The contract the composition induction consumes; discharged in Phase D. | Definition |
| (cascade-class predicate) | `RecoverableByDepth adj P bound` (in `CascadeOracle.lean`) вАФ Tier-1 (`recoverableByDepth_cfi`) / Tier-2 (`recoverableByDepth_scheme`) instances already proved. | (existing) |

### Phase C вАФ composition theorem

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `discrete_of_cellsAreOrbits_base` | 83-90 | **(C1) Finish.** At a base `T` where cells already coincide with `Aut_T`-orbits, warm refinement at `T` is `Discrete` вАФ the cascade reaching full canonization. | вАФ |
| `cellsAreOrbits_compose` | 92-105 | **(C2) Composition induction.** From layer 1's unconditional `CellsAreOrbits` at `T 0` and a `LayerStep` at each subsequent layer, `CellsAreOrbits` holds at the final cumulative set `T k`. | вАФ |
| `cumulative_card_le` | 107-113 | **Depths add (cardinality).** The cumulative individualization set `вЛГ_{iвЙ§k} S i` has size at most `ќ£_{iвЙ§k} f i` when each layer is bounded by its depth `f i`. | вАФ |
| `cascadeComposition` | 115-127 | **Theorem 3a (cascade composition) вАФ headline, conditional form.** Cumulative sets with layer-1 recoverability, per-layer transfer steps, and the final set a base вЯє warm refinement at `T k` reaches the discrete partition; with `cumulative_card_le` the cascade depth is `вЙ§ ќ£ fбµҐ`. Conditional on the `hstep` obligations (= ¬І4.2.5, Phase D). | вАФ |
| `cascadeComposition_single` | 135-138 | **Single-layer sanity check (k = 0).** One cascade-class layer that is a base reaches discreteness вАФ recovers the Tier-1/Tier-2 orbit-recovery theorems as the composition's base case. | вАФ |

### Phase D вАФ discharging `LayerStep` (the ¬І4.2.5 transfer), intrinsic route

Approach B (build-plan ¬І3): stay on `Fin n`, reduce `LayerStep` to a witness-upgrade via
**set-monotonicity** of warm refinement (reusing `refineStep_iff`); the materialized-quotient
route was rejected (`refineStep` axiomatic, no cross-size API).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `Refines ѕЗвВБ ѕЗвВВ` | `ѕЗвВБ` refines `ѕЗвВВ`: the partition of `ѕЗвВБ` is finer (`ѕЗвВБ a = ѕЗвВБ b вЖТ ѕЗвВВ a = ѕЗвВВ b`). The partition order used for warm-refinement monotonicity. | Definition |
| `signature_refines` | 156-177 | **Crux of warm-refinement monotonicity.** If `ѕЗвВБ` refines `ѕЗвВВ`, equal `ѕЗвВБ`-signatures give equal `ѕЗвВВ`-signatures, since `signature ѕЗвВВ` is the coarsening of `signature ѕЗвВБ`. | вАФ |
| `iterate_refineStep_refines` / `warmRefine_refines_initial` | warm refinement monotone in the initial colouring's partition order. | axiom-light |
| `individualizedColouring_refines` | 203-215 | Individualizing a superset gives a finer initial colouring: `T вКЖ T'` вЯє `individualizedColouring n T'` refines `individualizedColouring n T`. | вАФ |
| `warmRefine_indiv_mono` | 217-225 | **Set-monotonicity (the payoff).** Same `(T вИ™ S)`-cell вЯє same `T`-cell: 1-WL is monotone in the individualization set. The load-bearing lemma the docs had mis-cited as `warmRefine_refines`. | вАФ |
| `WitnessUpgrade adj P T S` | **The genuine ¬І4.2.5 content.** For `v, w` in the same `Aut_T`-orbit and the same `(T вИ™ S)`-cell, the orbit relation upgrades to `Aut_{TвИ™S}`. The Phase-D interface predicate. | Definition |
| `layerStep_of_witnessUpgrade` | 239-246 | **The reduction вАФ where Phase C meets the per-layer content.** A `WitnessUpgrade` discharges a `LayerStep`, via set-monotonicity then `CellsAreOrbits T` then the upgrade. | вАФ |
| `layerStep_empty` / `layerStep_subset` / `layerStep_of_cellsAreOrbits` / `layerStep_of_discrete` | Trivial real instances: no-op layer (`S = вИЕ`), `S вКЖ T`, independently-recoverable target, and the discretizing recursion-bottom. | axiom-light |
| `witnessUpgrade_of_pathFixing` | 271-286 | **Bridge to harvested generators.** If every same-orbit, same-cell pair admits a `P`-preserving automorphism whose support avoids `T вИ™ S` (fixes the committed path) and sends `v вЖ¶ w`, the witness-upgrade holds вАФ exactly what the cascade/linear oracles produce. | вАФ |

### Step 5 вАФ the synthesis (Theorem 3a reduced to harvested generators)

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `cascadeComposition_pathFixing` | 305-326 | **Theorem 3a, reduced to harvested path-fixing generators.** Cumulative sets by increments, layer-1 recoverable, every layer's residual symmetry realized by path-fixing automorphisms (`hwit`), and the final set a base вЯє discrete warm refinement at `T k`. Reduces all of Theorem 3a to the single hypothesis of per-layer path-fixing witness existence. | вАФ |
| `cascadeComposition_twoLayer` | 328-343 | **Smallest genuine composition.** An outer cascade-class layer at `TвВА`, an inner path-fixing layer with increment `S`, and the union a base вЯє discreteness вАФ the `CFI(scheme)` / `Scheme(CFI)` shape. | вАФ |

**Phase 6b вАФ CFI gadget flips discharge the Tier-3a `hwit`.** The Stage-3 gadget flip (`CFI.lean ¬І15`)
discharges `cascadeComposition_pathFixing`'s `hwit` for a CFI layering, conditional only on the per-layer
existence of committed-set-avoiding gadget flips (the cascade-1b content).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `CFILayerGadgetFlippable` | Per-layer CFI gadget-flip existence: for each layer and same-orbit/same-cell pair `(v,w)`, an even-symmetric cycle `F` whose flip maps `v вЖ¶ w` with `T i вИ™ S i` in `F`-free gadgets. The `hwit` analog of the linear oracle's `CFIGadgetFlippableLocal`. | Definition |
| `cfiLayer_pathFixing_hwit` | **The `hwit` drop-in.** `CFILayerGadgetFlippable` (+ `P` Aut-invariant) вЯє the Tier-3a `hwit` hypothesis, directly via `cfiFlipAut_pathFixing_witness`. | вАФ |

| `recoverableByDepth_of_pathFixing_layers` | 413-431 | **The harvest-window connector.** Lands `cascadeComposition_pathFixing`'s `Discrete` output onto the harvest `RecoverableByDepth` conclusion: a layer chain with per-layer path-fixing `hwit` and a base endpoint gives `RecoverableByDepth adj P b` at the chain-length bound. | вАФ |

| `ResidualAut` | 461-467 | **Residual automorphism.** A `P`-preserving automorphism of `adj` fixing `S` pointwise вАФ an element of the residual group `Aut_S^P`; the building block of the screen predicates. `OrbitPartition adj P S v w вЖФ вИГ ѕА, ResidualAut ѕА вИІ ѕА v = w`. | Definition |
| `ResidualAbelian` | 469-474 | **D2 вАФ abelian residual.** The residual group `Aut_S^P` is abelian (any two residual automorphisms commute) вАФ the screen's hidden-abelian / linear leg (calculator ¬І6); the `¬ђIsBase`-guarded form is the D2 disjunct. | Definition |
| `orbitPartition_iff_residualAut` | 476-482 | `OrbitPartition adj P S v w` unfolds to a `ResidualAut` carrying `v вЖ¶ w`. | вАФ |

| `residualAbelian_of_involutive` | 520-529 | **Exponent-2 вЯє abelian.** A residual group of involutions commutes вАФ wiring the abstract `ResidualAbelian` predicate to the precise `ResidualInvolutive`. | вАФ |
| `orbitPartition_swap_of_involutive` | 531-544 | **An involutive orbit witness is a swap.** With an exponent-2 residual, an `Aut_S`-orbit pair `a, b` has a residual automorphism with `g a = b` *and* `g b = a` вАФ closing the map-vs-swap gap class-agnostically (the content the CFI route obtains from gadget involutions). | вАФ |
| `swap_of_cellsAreOrbits_involutive` | 546-556 | **The class-agnostic swap certificate at a recoverable node.** Where orbit recovery holds (`CellsAreOrbits`) and the residual is exponent-2, every same-cell decision pair carries a swapping orbit automorphism вАФ the linear oracle's 'a swap exists' input from recovery + D2, replacing the per-class `CFIGadgetFlippable` derivation. | вАФ |
| `residualAut_eq_one_of_isBase` | 558-565 | Under a base (`IsBase`), every residual automorphism is the identity вАФ it can move no point. | вАФ |
| `residualAbelian_of_isBase` | 567-572 | **Trichotomy base case.** A trivial residual (under `IsBase`) is vacuously abelian, so `ResidualAbelian` holds at any base. | вАФ |
| `residualAbelian_mono` | 574-581 | **D2 inherited down the descent.** `ResidualAbelian` passes from `S` to any `S' вКЗ S` (the residual shrinks to a subgroup of an abelian group). | вАФ |
| `StabilizerAt` | 593-616 | **Part A (A1) вАФ the residual group `Aut_S^P` as a `Subgroup`.** Carrier the `P`-preserving automorphisms fixing `S` pointwise (`ResidualAut`); closure via `ResidualAut.mul`. The group object underlying the stabilizer chain. | Definition |

| `exists_greedy_base_aux` | 847-902 | **(A3.6 вАФ greedy-base existence, strong-induction core; step 2.1)** For every bound `N` on `|Aut_S^P|`, a base sequence `bs` from `S` with `2 ^ bs.length вЙ§ |Aut_S^P|`. | `orbitCoverage_of_blockDecomposition` | 1339-1359 | **(Route B Phase 1 core вАФ swap decomposition of orbit coverage)** The closure-based coverage of base point `b`'s full residual orbit factors, along a partition `ќ≤` (block system), into **block-reach** `hreach` (closure sends `b` into every orbit-mate's block) + **within-block coverage** `hfiber` (closure realizes same-block orbit pairs). | `coversOrbits_of_blockDecomposition` | 1375-1394 | **(Route B Phase 2 вАФ assemble coverage from per-level block decomposition)** Iterating `coversOrbits_cons_of_blockDecomposition` down a base sequence: per-level block-reach (`hreach`, quotient) + within-block coverage (`hfiber`, fiber) + terminal base вЯє `CoversOrbits adj P gens bs S`. | `reachesRigid_of_blockDecomposition` | 1396-1413 | **(Route B Phase 2 вАФ `ReachesRigid` from the block decomposition; the chain completed)** Per-level block-reach + within-block coverage + base вЯє `closure (gensAt вА¶ S) = StabilizerAt adj P S` (the harvest reproduces `Aut_S` = ReachesRigid). | `intraCellRelations_eq_singleton_zero_of_primitive` | 4668-4684 | **(The intra-cell route's boundary.)** For a *primitive* scheme and any base individualizing a point (`t вИИ SвВА`, `w вЙ† t`), `intraCellRelations S SвВА = {0}` identically: it's a `ClosedSubset` (`intraCellRelations_isClosed`) so primitivity forces `{0}`/`univ`, and `вЙ† univ` is free (`intraCellRelations_ne_univ_of_sep`). | `PersistentTwinGivesIntraCellBlock` | 4686-4700 | **(The sharpened open kernel вАФ G2-B isolated to nontriviality.)** Persistence (`¬ђ SeparatesAtBoundedBase`) вЯє large, or a bounded base whose `intraCellRelations` is `вЙ† {0}` and `вЙ† univ`. `PersistentTwinYieldsBlock` with the `ClosedSubset` construction (and `вЙ† univ`) discharged, so the *only* open content is nontriviality `вЙ† {0}` (a persistent twin gives a **whole** intra-cell non-diagonal relation, not one pair). ## ChainDescent/CoherentConfig.lean

The **general (multi-fiber) coherent-configuration substrate** вАФ Stage 0/1 of the general-CC
separability build (`docs/chain-descent-general-cc-separability.md`; Stage-0 decision + increment log
in its ¬І8). Lands the `CoherentConfig` type (colour-function presentation, fibers *derived*), the
homogeneous coercion, the general-CC `AlgIso`/`Separable` (the ¬ІS.17 widening the Stage-1.3 soundness
gate demanded), the probe-validated Thm 4.1 hypothesis predicates (`Theorem41ConditionsProbe.cs`),
the cited `Theorem41Statement` (the staging-fallback carry), and the point extension as a universal
property вАФ **plus its ¬ІCC.8 construction (Stage 1.2, 2026-06-12)**: the coherent closure
`pointExtension X T` via a pair-refinement saturation (setoid `pairStep`, representative-indexed
counts, `n¬≤`-round pigeonhole), discharging `IsPointExtension` constructively
(`isPointExtension_pointExtension` / `exists_isPointExtension` / `isPointExtension_unique`).
Axiom-clean `[propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound]`, no `sorry`.

| `CoherentConfig` | 48-74 | **The general (multi-fiber) coherent configuration** on `Fin n`, by its colour function `relOf : Fin n вЖТ Fin n вЖТ Fin rank` + four axioms (classes nonempty, transpose well-defined, reflexive classes purely diagonal, intersection numbers constant). The central missing object the live build creates; the point extension `X_T` (non-homogeneous) is why it exists. | Structure |

| `CoherentConfig.confusionMultiplicity` | 2627-2634 | ¬ІCC.22c (D1, route ¬І9.6) **The confusion multiplicity (cover-load) of a vertex** вАФ the number of big confusion *pairs* `(ќ±,ќ≤)` (`ќ±вЙ†ќ≤`, `c(X)<2¬Ј|C(ќ±,ќ≤)|`) that `v` fails to distinguish (`vвИИC(ќ±,ќ≤)`). | `CoherentConfig.confusionMultiplicity_perm` | 2636-2675 | ¬ІCC.22c (D1, the multiplicity punchline) **Confusion multiplicity is a CC-automorphism invariant.** `confusionMultiplicity (ѕА v) = confusionMultiplicity v` for a `relOf`-preserving `ѕА`: the product map `(ќ±,ќ≤)вЖ¶(ѕАќ±,ѕАќ≤)` bijects the big pairs `v` lies in onto those `ѕАv` lies in (`big_confusion_perm`+`mem_confusionSet_perm`+injectivity).
